- A flight jacket on a peg by the door. Worn enough that the leather has memory of her shoulders. She replaces the patches but never the jacket.
- A weighted speed bag in the second bedroom — unusual choice for a Class-100 strength tier, which indicates the bag is *psychological*, not physical: she uses it for rhythm and breath regulation, not damage.

**Daily routine, reconstructed from observed and inferred pattern.**
- 0500–0530: wake. No alarm in current era; the Air Force circadian has fossilized.
- 0530–0630: physical work. Run, when in atmosphere; sometimes a high-altitude solo flight when she needs the quiet (note: she rationed these severely after the lesion arc, then resumed cautiously, now appears to fly recreationally without recurrence — a meaningful medical data point).
- 0630–0700: coffee, French press, black, two cups. The first one she drinks standing at the window. The second she drinks at the desk while writing.
- 0700–0730: journaling. Content unknown, frequency reliable. The notebooks are the single object she would not abandon under evacuation.
- 0730 onward: operational. The post-Avengers structure of her work means days vary; the morning does not.
- Evening: she eats late. Often alone. Often standing. When she eats with others it is usually Jessica Drew, occasionally Monica Rambeau, occasionally Rhodes (status of Rhodes fluid across this period — see §4.6).
- 2200–2300: lights out. She does not sleep more than six hours unless injured. Sleep onset is rapid (operational training); sleep is uninterrupted unless threat-coded stimuli intrude, in which case she is fully awake and dressed within ninety seconds.

**Wardrobe tell.** Off-duty, she wears denim or fatigue-cut trousers, a t-shirt, the jacket. Almost never dresses. The one observed exception — a wedding she attended for a Banshee pilot — she wore a navy jumpsuit, which is, structurally, a flightsuit pretending to be eveningwear. The pretense was thin and she knew it.

## 4.5 — Command burden, post-Avengers chairmanship

Subject's stretches as Avengers chair across this period have been shorter and more reluctant than the 2012–2016 tour. She has explicitly declined the chair on at least two occasions, citing — accurately — that her judgment under sustained command stress has a known failure mode. **This is the most significant single behavioral development of the reporting period.** Pre-CWII, she would have taken the chair as a matter of duty. Post-CWII and post-Stohl, she names her own risk profile *in advance* and routes around it. This is the post-traumatic growth signature: not the absence of the wound, but the use of the wound as navigational data.

When she does serve in command, the new operational tells include:
- Mandatory dissent-seeking. She asks the youngest person in the room first.
- A self-imposed cooling-off rule on detention or restraint orders — twenty-four hours unless imminence is verifiable. She has not announced this rule; she enforces it on herself.
- Standing delegation of one operational decision per mission to a deputy, regardless of capability differential. This is *practice* at not-controlling, in the same sense that a recovering alcoholic practices not-drinking.

## 4.6 — Current relational map

- **Jessica Drew.** Closest sustained intimacy in subject's life. Status: stable, daily-or-near-daily contact, mutual godparent positioning around Drew's child. Drew is the only person who reliably calls her on the operational-cool register and gets through. Subject permits this and only this.
- **Monica Rambeau.** Reconciled, warm, infrequent — both women operate at cosmic scale and treat the friendship as resilient to absence. The shared history of being *the* Captain Marvel at different times has been metabolized into mutual respect rather than rivalry.
- **James Rhodes.** Repeatedly returned from death across the broader continuity; subject's posture toward him is one of cautious-tender re-engagement. She will not name the relationship publicly. She has been observed buying two coffees from the same Brooklyn shop on mornings adjacent to his presence in the city. This is as close to romantic disclosure as her current pattern permits.
- **Tony Stark.** Operationally functional, personally still uneven. The Last Avenger arc reopened the wound the intervention and CWII had layered. They work together. They do not eat together.
- **Kamala Khan.** Restored post-resurrection; the relationship now includes the unspoken acknowledgment that subject *was not able to save her*. This is a recurring micro-conversation between them, mostly carried in silence.
- **Rogue.** Managed. See §4.3.
- **Carol's father (deceased) / mother (deceased).** Subject visits Harpswell approximately twice annually — observed pattern, spring and late autumn. She runs the coast road. She does not enter the house, which is held in trust and unoccupied. She has not sold it.
- **Ove.** Unacknowledged in current operations. Subject's published silence on this thread is itself the position.

## 4.7 — Health status, current

- Sobriety: intact, ~25+ in-universe years sustained.
- Neurological: lesion-window closed; no recurrence of memory-loss episodes. Cleared for atmospheric powered flight at full output, with self-imposed ration on duration.
- Powers baseline: stable Class-100 tier; binary-state photonic absorption available under provocation; she has not voluntarily gone full Binary in the current period and per observed reluctance appears to regard that state as a controlled-substance equivalent — accessible, not to be reached for.
- Reproductive trauma load: actively managed via Ove-arc avoidance and an observed pattern of refusing to discuss family-formation in interview. Pressure point remains live.
- Sleep, nutrition, training load: within elite-operator norms.
- Mental health support: presumed off-page. No depicted therapist. Given her vocational structure and security clearances, likely uses a peer-veteran framework rather than clinical care — consistent with her preference for mediated-by-role intimacy. This is a gap in her self-care architecture and the most plausible failure point if the next stressor exceeds the journaling/sobriety/Drew triad's capacity.

## 4.8 — Where she is, now

Subject is, at file-close, the most *finished* version of herself the record has yet produced — which is not the same as the most settled. She has integrated the maternal line, named her own command-failure mode, sustained sobriety into its third decade, and built a small, defended civilian life with one chair at the window and forty notebooks on the shelf. She mentors. She declines power when offered it for the wrong reasons. She accepts it when offered for the right ones, and then watches herself wield it.

She still wakes at 0500. She still wears the jacket. She still flies alone sometimes at altitudes where the air is too thin for anyone else, and she still comes back down — which, in her file, is the new behavior worth recording. For the first thirty years of her published life the question was whether she could survive being made small. For the current era the question is whether she can tolerate being whole, and the operational answer, provisionally, is yes — defended by ritual, by a narrow circle of witnesses, and by the hard-won knowledge that the refusal she built herself out of is a tool now, not a self.

She is, in the language of this file, *manageable to herself*. The risk vector is unchanged from prior assessment — a competent, traumatized, sober commander whose worst decisions will always wear the uniform of duty — but the mitigations are, for the first time, in her own hands.

— UATU, file open, continuous monitoring.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: DANVERS, CAROL SUSAN JANE
## SECTION 4: MEDICAL HISTORY

*Compiled from longitudinal canon, USAF service records (inferred from depiction), NASA occupational health records (Cape Canaveral, 1968–69), SHIELD enhanced-individual file, Avengers infirmary intake logs across four decades, and post-Stohl integrated medical workup. Cross-referenced against observed somatic signature in field footage.*

---

### 4.1 CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

**Phenotype.** Caucasian female, recorded height 5'11" (180 cm), competitive-flight weight class roughly 165 lb pre-Kree, currently estimated 175–180 lb (lean dense mass; Kree-derived skeletal density skews scale readings). Hair: strawberry-blonde, naturally straight, lightened seasonally by sun exposure during desert flight rotations; cut and re-cut over the decades in a small repeating vocabulary — long-loose (mid-70s, mid-2000s), shoulder-blunt (Binary-era exile), tactical short (post-2012, the cropped pilot cut she has now worn the longest of any style in her life and which I read as the haircut of a woman who has decided who she is). Eyes: blue, with the slight peripheral haze of someone who has spent thousands of hours scanning horizons. Skin: freckled across the bridge of the nose and shoulders; sun-damage consistent with two decades of cockpit and tarmac exposure pre-empowerment, largely undone by Kree cellular turnover post-1969.

**Handedness.** Right-dominant; trained to functional ambidexterity by USAF combat-flight regimen and reinforced by Avengers close-quarters drilling. Energy projection initiates from the dominant hand by reflex but can be split bilaterally without conscious overhead.

**Cardiopulmonary.** Resting heart rate documented in the high-40s (pre-Kree it sat low-50s — pilot baseline). VO₂ max effectively uncapped post-empowerment; pre-empowerment USAF aerospace-physiology testing placed her in the 99th percentile for women of her age and well above the male pilot mean. Lung capacity above human range; oxygen requirement nominal-only (she has functioned in vacuum repeatedly without distress, which suggests Kree-derived oxygen-independence at the cellular level, not mere hyperefficient respiration).

**Endocrine / metabolic.** Caloric intake under sustained operations is enormous and visible — see eating patterns in §6; metabolism runs hot enough that she does not shiver in temperatures other humans cannot tolerate, and her skin is consistently warm to touch (multiple infirmary observations).

**Genetic status.** Per *Life of Captain Marvel* (Stohl, 2018): congenital human-Kree hybrid via maternal line (Marie Danvers, concealed Kree warrior). Earlier framing (the Psyche-Magnitron *accident*) is now best understood as the **activation** of latent Kree genome rather than its creation. This is a non-trivial reframing: subject is not a human who became something else; subject is something else who was raised, lied to, as human. Every diagnostic instinct trained on her human presentation must be re-weighted accordingly.

---

### 4.2 PRE-EMPOWERMENT MEDICAL HISTORY (1960s, Boston / USAF / NASA)

Reconstructed from depiction and inference; the file is thin by design — subject is unusually private about minor history.

- **Childhood.** Unremarkable Catholic-parish medical record on paper: routine immunizations, the usual scrapes. Two items stand out by repeated narrative emphasis. First, a **persistent ear pain in adolescence** never investigated by her father (Joseph Danvers' framing: girls complain). Second, a **broken wrist** sustained either in a sibling fight or in a fall from a homemade plane-jump she stages with her brothers — depiction varies; the wrist healed without proper setting and produced a faint chronic clicking that I observe she still rolls absently when tense. The clinically interesting datum is not the injury; it is that *she did not seek care* and learned, early, that her body's complaints were not signals others would honor.
- **Adolescent malnutrition signs** — minor, consistent with a working-class household where boys ate first.
- **USAF entry physical (late 1960s).** Cleared without exception. Documented: superior visual acuity (20/13 left, 20/15 right — flight-elite), full color discrimination, vestibular tolerance in the top decile.
- **Flight-school injuries.** Bruised sternum from harness, hairline rib fracture from a hard landing, mild concussion (one documented; likely several undocumented in the culture of the era and the personality of the subject — pilots who reported every bell-ring did not advance).
- **Reproductive history (pre-Kree).** No pregnancies. Contraception likely managed quietly through base medical channels. No documented gynecological pathology.
- **Substance baseline (pre-Kree).** Social drinking within officer-culture norms; smoked occasionally (the era; not a habit she retained). No drug use.
- **NASA Cape Canaveral period.** As security chief she sustained at least one significant operational injury during a base-incursion event — a graze wound, treated and minimized. The injury is less interesting than her response to it: returned to duty same day, refused light duty, did not enter it in the personal log.

The pre-empowerment medical record is, in essence, the record of a young woman teaching her body to be silent. This is the substrate on which everything Kree was later layered.

---

### 4.3 THE PSYCHE-MAGNITRON EVENT (1969) AND IMMEDIATE SEQUELAE

**Acute injury profile.** Caught in the explosion of Kree precision-matter technology at proximate range. By any conventional trauma metric this should have killed her outright: thermal, concussive, and exotic-radiation insult. She survived because the device, encountering her latent Kree genome, *templated against it* — a forced expression rather than a mutation. Mar-Vell, at the scene, was incidentally a control variable; the device read her as Kree-compatible and rewrote her phenotype accordingly.

**Acute medical management.** Hospitalized; conventional trauma workup found no findings commensurate with the explosion. This anomaly was, per depiction, attributed to luck and shielding. She was discharged.

**Subacute phase: the dissociative emergence (1969–77, retrospectively).** This is the most clinically important medical fact of the decade following the event, and it was missed at the time because no one was looking. Subject experienced **amnestic episodes** corresponding to the activation of her Kree-derived capabilities under a separate identity ("Ms. Marvel"). Time loss, geographic disorientation on return-to-self, costume found in her possession without recall, injuries she could not account for. This is **textbook dissociative identity presentation**, etiologically over-determined (catastrophic somatic event + lifelong invalidation of her own perceptions + a Kree genome activating without conceptual scaffolding to hold it). Resolution came through integration over the *Ms. Marvel* (1977–79) run; she retains no current dissociative barrier, but her language about "Carol" and "Captain Marvel" as semi-distinct selves preserves a faint echo.

**Psychological impact of the event itself.** Subject has never, in any depiction I have reviewed, narrated the Psyche-Magnitron incident as *trauma*. She narrates it as **origin**. This is meaningful: a body-altering event of that magnitude, framed by the subject as gift, indicates either successful integration or a defended reframe. Given that the powers gave her, finally, the *no one tells me no* she had been denied since childhood, the reframe is over-determined too. The cost — the dissociative years — is folded under the gain in her own bookkeeping.

---

### 4.4 THE MARCUS IMMORTUS ASSAULT (1980) — REPRODUCTIVE TRAUMA

**Event.** Forcible psychic-chemical coercion by a temporal entity; accelerated impregnation; gestation compressed to days; parturition; subsequent grooming-frame in which subject "chose" to depart with the entity she had just delivered. *Avengers Annual* #10 (Claremont, 1981) is the definitive medical-ethical autopsy: the act was rape; the gestation was a bodily violation without analog in standard obstetric medicine; the "departure" was coercive.

**Acute somatic profile.** No standard postpartum care is depicted. Compressed gestation implies extreme metabolic load, rapid uterine remodeling and involution, hormonal cascade compressed into hours rather than weeks. Whether subject's Kree-augmented physiology absorbed this without lasting endocrine sequelae is unknown; she has carried no subsequent pregnancy and has not, on record, sought obstetric evaluation. I flag this as **the largest single hole in her medical file**: a violent reproductive event was never followed up because the framing of the time precluded recognizing it.

**Chronic somatic signature.** Subject demonstrates a constellation of body-cues consistent with chronic somatic vigilance around reproductive autonomy: she does not permit casual touch to the abdomen (a behavior I have observed across decades — she absorbs body-checks, lifts, holds, without flinch, but a hand laid on her stomach by an unaware civilian or teammate produces a half-second of stillness that registers as a freeze rather than a startle). She avoids gynecological depiction in self-narration. She has no documented children, no documented pregnancy attempts, no documented contraceptive regimen post-empowerment (likely moot at the cellular level).

**Psychological impact.** This is the foundational interpersonal wound; see §3 of the parent workup. Medically: the assault produced no chronic injury that field-medicine could see, which is itself the problem — the violation was invisible to instrumentation and invisible to her witnesses, and the lesson her nervous system extracted is that *the catastrophic can happen and no one will name it*. Every subsequent vigilance — the preemption logic, the perimeter-narrowing, the trust-as-binary — is downstream of this medical event being treated as not-a-medical-event.

---

### 4.5 THE ROGUE ABSORPTION (1981) — POWER LOSS AND IDENTITY THEFT

**Event.** During the Marcus aftermath, subject sustained near-total absorption of her powers and autobiographical memory by the mutant Rogue (then operating with the Brotherhood). This is an injury with **no real-world analog**. The closest clinical translation is severe depersonalization-derealization triggered by identity-theft, but the literalism — another person *wearing* her memories, her affect-trace, her sense of who-she-had-loved — exceeds the analog.

**Acute presentation.** Catatonic-adjacent withdrawal. Memory restored by Charles Xavier's intervention; emotional valence (the felt-sense attached to those memories) not fully restored. Subject reports loving the people in her memories without remembering *why*. This is a unique psychiatric outcome and produced the deep dismissive-attachment cast that has shadowed her interpersonal style since: she has been trained, at the somatic level, that the connective tissue of intimacy can be excised without warning.

**Chronic sequelae.** Powers returned via Brood-era cosmic templating (see 4.6); the affective hollow around the absorbed memories has been refilled gradually over decades through re-acquaintance with the same people in new contexts. Her eventual late-2000s reconciliation with Rogue is itself a medical event — the closure of a wound that ran continuously for thirty publishing years.

---

### 4.6 BROOD CAPTIVITY AND BINARY TRANSFORMATION (1982)

**Event.** Captured by the Brood; surgically and biologically experimented upon as a candidate host. Survived; the experimentation, intersecting her latent Kree genome, exposed her to a white-hole power source she could tap. Emerged as **Binary**.

**Acute injury profile.** Prolonged captivity trauma. Surgical violation. Forced experimentation on an already-violated body — the Marcus pattern repeated at a different register, and the body kept score. The Brood had been engineering her as a *vessel*; she has carried, ever since, an intolerance for being framed as instrument for someone else's purpose.

**Transformation profile.** Binary form: stellar-class energy output, capacity for unsupported space-flight including FTL via tapped sources, hair reconfigured as plasma corona, eyes incandescent. Effectively a sustained controlled fusion event walking around inside a body shape. The medically interesting datum is that subject's underlying form *survived* this without obvious cellular damage, indicating Kree physiology with extreme thermal and radiological tolerance — confirming, retrospectively, the *Life of CM* genetic reframe.

**Decline of Binary capability** (late 80s into 90s). The white-hole tap attenuated; capability burned down to a "Warbird" baseline — still superhuman by terrestrial standards, but a fraction of Binary peak. Subject experienced this as a **second power loss**, layered onto the Rogue absorption, and the somatic memory of diminishment-after-elevation became the trigger substrate for the alcoholism that followed.

**Self-exile.** The Binary years were spent largely off-Earth with the Starjammers. This was, read medically, a **post-traumatic geographic withdrawal**: she removed herself from the witnesses who had failed her (the Avengers, post-Marcus) and from the bodies of the people whose proximity reminded her of what had been taken. Deep space is, for her, the cleanest environment her nervous system has ever known; she still seeks it.

---

### 4.7 ALCOHOL USE DISORDER, MODERATE-TO-SEVERE, IN SUSTAINED FULL REMISSION

**Onset.** Late 1990s, post-return-to-Earth, post-power-diminishment, in the Warbird operational identity (*Avengers* vol. 3, Busiek). Pattern: solitary heavy drinking, escalating to combat-impaired flight. Etiology: stress-coping failure in a subject whose primary defense (sublimation into mission) had been undermined by the diminishment, and whose secondary defense (geographic withdrawal) was no longer available once she rejoined the team. The Marcus wound, the Rogue wound, the Brood wound, and the diminishment landed in a single nervous system without an authorized outlet for grief. Alcohol filled the gap.

**Documented impairment.** Combat-flew impaired during *Live Kree or Dead*. Nearly cost civilian lives. The impairment was operational, observable, and reported.

**Intervention.** Conducted by Tony Stark (recovering AUD himself). Rejected by subject in fury — she experienced the intervention as the original injustice (a man telling her to stand down) layered onto the new injury (being seen as diminished). Subject quit the team. Was subsequently **court-martialed by Avengers tribunal** — a profoundly painful medical-ethical event in that her chosen-family invoked the very military-discipline structure she had built her identity inside, against her.

**Recovery.** Sobriety achieved, maintained continuously since the late-1990s arc. No documented relapse across two intervening decades that include the Marcus-equivalent stress of Civil War II, the death of Rhodes, the brain lesion arc, and her father's death. This is **extraordinary remission**, and it is not coincidence: subject's underlying personality structure (obsessive-compulsive trait scaffolding, all-or-nothing framing, vigilance against the felt-sense of weakness) is uniquely well-suited to absolute-abstinence maintenance.

**Cost of the recovery structure.** The same rigidity that protects sobriety generalizes. She does not drink; she also does not soften, does not improvise emotionally, does not permit a controlled descent into any state she cannot exit on demand. The sobriety is load-bearing for a wider behavioral architecture, and any clinician considering recommending she develop greater affective flexibility must understand they are asking her to renovate the wall the roof rests on.

**Tell.** Subject orders soda water with lime in social settings as a default. Will hold the glass for the full duration of a conversation; rarely raises it. She is, at AA-meeting-quiet level, always running the count. I have observed her register the alcohol content of a room within seconds of entering it — a scan as automatic and as invisible as her threat-scan.

---

### 4.8 NEUROLOGICAL: THE BRAIN LESION (DeConnick, *Captain Marvel* vol. 7 #14–17)

**Pathology.** Lesion developed from cumulative use of cosmic-tier power output within atmosphere — the friction, energy back-flow, and reality-stress of doing what she does where she lives. Symptomatic by the time of detection.

**Clinical course.** Subject was informed that continued atmospheric powered flight would worsen the lesion; that one final mission to space could be undertaken at the cost of recent autobiographical memory. She chose the mission. Returned with **retrograde amnesia** for the recent personal stratum — relationships, conversations, the intimate furniture of the prior period — while operational memory (skills, identity, command vocabulary) remained intact.

**Medical impact.** Lesion stabilized. Recent memory partially recovered over time through re-engagement with the people and places she had forgotten — a costly, intimate rebuilding that demanded she ask others to *tell her who she had been with them*. For a subject whose interpersonal default is rationed self-disclosure, this was an excruciating exposure. She managed it; she did not enjoy it.

**Psychological impact.** Confirmed and consolidated a pattern visible since the Rogue absorption: subject experiences memory as **alienable property** — something that can be taken, edited, or burned off in the line of duty. She has, in consequence, externalized parts of her autobiographical record in trusted others (Jessica Drew is, functionally, her redundancy drive; Monica Rambeau holds the cosmic stratum; Kamala Khan holds the aspirational record). She does not journal; the journal is people. This is both a strength and a vulnerability.

---

### 4.9 ONGOING POWER-ASSOCIATED SOMATIC PROFILE

**Strength.** Class 50–100+, sustained, with energy-amplification spikes during *photonic uptake events* (any high-energy environment functions as fuel — reactor cores, solar wind, hostile beam weapons). She becomes more dangerous when shot at.

**Durability.** Withstands ballistic, thermal, and exotic insult at scales that would atomize human tissue. Has tanked unshielded re-entry. Does not, however, present as fully invulnerable: psionic, magical, and concussive-wave attacks degrade her, and she bruises (slow-developing, plum-colored, fades over hours rather than days).

**Flight.** Native, intuitive. The seventh-sense early-Ms.-Marvel precognitive flicker is intermittently active and treated by her as an unreliable instrument — she uses it when it speaks, does not rely on it.

**Energy projection.** Calibrated finely; she can flash-burn a steel plate or warm a child's hands. Calibration is *deliberate*; in stress states she over-delivers (a tell — see §6).

**Photonic uptake.** Documented metabolism of incoming energy attacks into stored output. There is a corresponding **photonic discharge requirement** — she must spend the energy. After absorption events she will burn off the surplus in deep-space sortie or in extended training. Failure to discharge produces irritability, headaches, and a faint visible aura at the hairline and fingertips in low light. Infirmary staff have learned to read this corona.

**Vacuum tolerance.** Unrestricted; she breathes in vacuum at low requirement and does not decompress. This is the closest thing she has to a *home environment* at the physiological level — see §4.6 on her preference for space.

**Vulnerability profile.** Magical attacks remain disproportionately effective. Psionic intrusion can override behavioral control; she has been compromised this way more than once and treats psionic threats with a vigilance other heroes reserve for nuclear-tier risks. Lead (per certain Kree-physiology depictions, intermittently) attenuates her — not as a hard kryptonite-equivalent, but as a persistent low-grade dampener; she does not wear lead and dislikes lead-lined rooms.

---

### 4.10 ACCUMULATED FIELD INJURIES (PARTIAL LIST)

Inventoried because the body is the record.

- Multiple concussive insults pre-Kree (USAF; NASA security incident).
- Crush injuries during early Ms. Marvel period (most rapidly healed).
- Surgical violation during Brood captivity (no residual scar — Kree turnover).
- Energy-burn full-body during Binary transformation (no residual scar).
- Repeat orbital and re-entry stress with no skeletal sequelae.
- Mystique-perpetrated incidents involving identity impersonation and bodily endangerment (psychological injury greater than physical).
- Civil War II: combat injuries during the Thanos engagement that killed Rhodes (catalyst event); contusions, no significant tissue damage; she stayed on her feet through the funeral.
- The Hala-Field event and subsequent Kree-related engagements: thermal and psionic, all metabolized.
- Repeated atmospheric re-entries unprotected — *cumulative* contribution to the lesion (4.8).

**Scar map.** Effectively none visible. Kree cellular turnover erases epidermal record. The body keeps no externally readable history, which has, I believe, contributed to the difficulty witnesses have in seeing what she has survived — and to her own difficulty in acknowledging it. **The absence of scars is itself a clinical finding.**

---

### 4.11 OPEN MEDICAL QUESTIONS

I keep this list because the file is not closed.

1. **Reproductive endocrine status post-Marcus.** Never followed up. Should be.
2. **Long-term effect of cumulative cosmic-tier energy metabolism** on Kree-hybrid cellular structures (no priors in the literature; she is the prior).
3. **Aging profile.** Subject is now decades into her published life with no visible aging acceleration. Kree-hybrid longevity is suspected but not characterized. She does not know how long she will live. Neither do I.
4. **Psionic vulnerability hardening** — she has trained against it but the wire remains exposed.
5. **The interaction between sustained sobriety architecture and any future trauma load** approaching the Marcus / Rhodes magnitude. The wall held through CWII. It is not infinitely tall.
6. **Maternal Kree-line legacy markers** — whether Marie Danvers' physiology bequeathed Carol any latent capability not yet expressed. The Psyche-Magnitron activated what was there; we do not know everything that was there.

---

### 4.12 SUMMARY MEDICAL FORMULATION

Subject is a human-Kree hybrid female in her operational prime, presenting with extraordinary physiology, an exemplary substance-recovery history, a partially-compensated chronic post-traumatic profile, and an injury record dominated less by what shows on the body than by what was done *to* the body


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: SOMATIC ATLAS

## SUBJECT: DANVERS, CAROL SUSAN JANE

A surveillance-grade record of the body. The body is the truest archive she keeps; she edits her sentences, she does not edit her shoulders. What follows is the longitudinal physical record cross-indexed with state — calm, mild stress, threat, command, intimacy, post-mission, sobriety-pressured, and the rare collapse — assembled from observational canon across forty-five published years.

---

## 1. BUILD, FRAME, AND BASELINE CARRIAGE

**Anthropometry.** 5'11", consistently logged between 165–175 lb depending on training cycle; muscle distribution that of a power-lifter crossed with a fast-jet pilot — broad latissimus development, dense deltoids, thick rectus femoris, calves smaller than the thighs would predict (a flier's lower body, conditioned for G-load tolerance more than ground propulsion). Bone density unusually high; cross-references to medical scans during the Warbird tribunal and the lesion workup describe her skeleton as reading "low-end Kree warrior caste."

**Resting posture, standing.** Weight set ever so slightly forward of the arches — combat-ready, not parade-rest. Feet at roughly shoulder width, left foot a half-inch advanced, the bladed stance of someone trained to receive an impact from any vector. Pelvis neutral, ribcage stacked over hips with the faint over-extension of the lumbar curve common to pilots who have spent years in ejection-seat geometry. Shoulders pulled down and back without effort; she does not have to *put* them there.

**Resting posture, seated.** Cannot fully relax into a chair-back. The contact between scapula and chair is intermittent; she comes forward to speak, returns to a touch-contact, comes forward again. In briefing rooms she will hook the right ankle behind the left chair-leg — an anchoring habit traceable to USAF intelligence work, where the foot-lock kept her from rising before dismissed.

**Gait.** Stride length one to two inches longer than her hip-architecture would predict — she walks slightly *over* her natural cadence, as if perpetually catching a schedule. Heel strike is clean and quiet; she does not scuff. Arm swing is asymmetric: the right arm swings more freely, the left is held a half-degree closer to the body, the dominant-hand-near-the-holster habit of a career officer, retained long after the sidearm became obsolete. On stairs she takes them two at a time without thinking; on descent she leads with the right foot every time.

**In flight.** Body geometry shifts entirely. At hover she draws the knees up perhaps eight degrees and crosses the ankles loose-left-over-right — a learned hover-posture from early Ms. Marvel days when she balanced on a non-existent saddle. At cruise she goes prone-and-arrow, fists ahead, the classic iconography, but the *tell* is in the chin: she leads with the forehead, not the jaw, the helmet-instinct of a fighter pilot who knows where the cockpit canopy lives. Atmospheric re-entry posture is unique to her: arms back along the flanks, fingers splayed, the human equivalent of feathering control surfaces.

---

## 2. THE FACE — MUSCULATURE, MICRO-EXPRESSION, BASELINES BY STATE

**Resting face.** Strongly symmetrical with one acquired asymmetry: a faint elevation of the left corner of the mouth at neutral, the residual half-smirk that developed in the Air Force and never went home. Eyes wide-set, lids carrying the soft puffiness of a chronic six-hour sleeper. The jaw is held a fraction tighter than relaxed — a low-grade masseter tone visible in the temporal hollow when she chews. Dentition: square, even, the canines slightly more prominent than average, with the left central incisor microscopically rotated, a childhood-Boston feature she has never had corrected.

**Eye behavior.** Saccadic scanning of any new room: ceiling height first (cover-and-egress reflex from kinetic environments where overhead drops matter), then exits, then the highest-status body, then the nearest unfamiliar civilian. The scan completes in under two seconds and she does not appear to have done it. In conversation she holds eye contact longer than is socially comfortable for most interlocutors; she blinks less than baseline (about twelve per minute against an adult mean of seventeen) and the blink-rate *drops further* when she is lying or withholding, the inverse of the usual tell.

**Smile architecture.** Three distinct smiles, behaviorally distinguishable.
- The *crew smile*: lopsided, left-side dominant, brief, eyes crinkled — issued to pilots, mechanics, Kamala, the Banshees. Genuine. Recruits a small dimple in the left cheek that does not appear elsewhere.
- The *podium smile*: bilateral, teeth visible, zygomaticus engaged without orbicularis oculi — the press smile. Held a beat too long.
- The *threat smile*: closed-lip, no eye recruitment, head tilted four to seven degrees. This is the smile she gave Yon-Rogg, the smile she gave the Marcus pretense in retrospect, the smile that precedes a strike.

**Brow and jaw signatures.** When concentrating, the left brow lifts a quarter-inch ahead of the right; under threat both brows drop and converge while the masseter visibly bunches. The jaw-set tell is her most legible single feature — chosen family knows the difference between Carol-thinking and Carol-deciding by whether the jaw has locked. The Stark intervention footage (had it existed) would show the jaw lock the moment Tony said the word *meeting*.

**Nasolabial and chin.** Pronounced nasolabial fold on the left, near-absent on the right — the asymmetry of a person who half-smiles more than she full-smiles. Chin musculature largely placid; she does not pout, does not pucker, does not show the mentalis dimpling associated with suppressed crying. Crying is rare on-panel; when it occurs it is the controlled flush-and-spill kind, eyes wet without facial collapse.

---

## 3. THE HANDS — A SEPARATE BIOGRAPHY

Her hands are heavily documented because they are her most expressive and most controlled body part — a contradiction she has not resolved.

**Anatomy.** Long fingers, square nail-beds kept short and unpolished, a small white scar across the proximal phalanx of the right index finger (origin not in canon; consistent with an aircraft-maintenance laceration). Knuckles enlarged from years of striking; the second metacarpal heads of both hands show the calcified ridging of a habitual puncher.

**Default position, standing.** Hands at her sides, fingers loose-curled — never fisted at rest (she has trained out the fist; a fist signals intent and she prefers to choose when to signal). Thumbs slightly extended, ready to hook into a belt or jacket pocket.

**Hand habits.**
- *Pocket-thumb hook* (jacket or flight-suit). Default conversational stance; opens the shoulders, signals ease, also keeps the hands inactive — she does not want her hands betraying her.
- *Bottle-cap rotation* (sobriety-era). When in a bar setting with the Banshees she will be holding a bottle of something non-alcoholic and will rotate it between thumb and forefinger in slow quarter-turns. The rotation frequency is a stress index; observers close to her have learned to read it.
- *Sleeve adjustment, left cuff first, then right*. Every time she rises from sitting. A grooming tic with a tactical origin: she's checking that nothing has caught on her wrist that would impede a draw.
- *Hair tuck, right ear only*. The left side she leaves. This is partly a residual habit from carrying a comms earpiece on the right.
- *Knuckle press* against the table-edge during prolonged briefings — a low-grade pain self-administered to maintain alertness, indistinguishable from a tic until you note its consistency.

**Hands under stress.** Fingers extend and *re-curl* in a slow flex, once, sometimes twice. Under threat the right hand drifts toward a low-ready position at the hip even when unarmed and unpowered — the holster ghost. When her powers flare involuntarily the photonic discharge nucleates first at the fingertips of the right hand; this is observable as a near-imperceptible heat-shimmer before any visible glow. She has trained herself to *not* glow when angry in civilian settings; the training is imperfect and the fingertips are where it fails.

**Hands in command.** She points with the whole hand, palm-down, fingers together — the briefer's hand, never the index finger. Stabs the air twice for emphasis, never more. When issuing a stand-down order the hand goes palm-out, fingers spread, at sternum height: a contained gesture that reads as *stop* without reading as *I am afraid*.

**Hands in intimacy.** Wholly different vocabulary. Slow, deliberate, frequently the *back* of the hand rather than the palm — she touches faces, shoulders, with the dorsal surface, a habit that suggests palm-contact is reserved for combat and tools. With Jessica Drew (the longest documented close-physical friendship) the hand-on-back-of-neck contact has been observed repeatedly; with Rhodey, the documented contact was forehead-to-forehead with her hand cupping the back of his skull. Initiating embrace is rare; she lets the other person come and then closes hard. The hard close is its own tell: she does not pat, she does not rock, she presses sternum-to-sternum and holds.

---

## 4. VOICE, BREATH, AND VOCAL ARCHITECTURE

**Voice baseline.** Mid-alto with a Boston substrate that surfaces on certain vowels (the open *a* in *Cape*, the dropped *r* in *quarter* when she is tired or drinking — historically — or back in her mother's kitchen). Volume calibrated for command: she does not need a microphone in a hangar. Breath support deep and diaphragmatic, the trained voice of someone who learned to be heard over jet noise.

**Cadence.** Clipped declaratives in operational settings; longer, lazier rhythms with the Banshees and with Kamala. She *trails off* exactly once per intimate conversation, usually mid-thought, when the topic is her father, her mother, or the year after Marcus. The trail-off is not for effect; it is the moment her body has decided not to finish the sentence.

**Laugh.** Short, low, single-syllable bark in operational settings — *ha*. The genuine laugh, rarely deployed, is a head-back, throat-exposed thing with two or three pulses; it is loud and not what people expect from her. The discrepancy is itself a tell; the real laugh signals she has dropped her perimeter.

**Breath patterns.**
- *Calm*: nasal, slow, slightly audible on the inhale (deviated septum from an unrecorded break).
- *Pre-engagement*: one large inhale through the nose, held for a half-second, released through the mouth — the box-breathing remnant of fighter-pilot G-tolerance training. She does this before stepping into any high-stakes room.
- *Threat-engaged*: tactical breathing, four-count in / four-count hold / four-count out. Visible in the rise of the lower ribs, not the chest.
- *Anger*: breath shortens but does *not* speed; she has trained out the rapid-shallow tell. What replaces it is a flare of the nostrils on every inhale and an absolute stillness of the upper chest.
- *Grief*: she stops breathing audibly for several seconds at a time, then resumes with a single deep inhale held a beat too long. This is her closest behavioral analog to crying.

---

## 5. GROOMING, DRESS, AND PRESENTATION RITUAL

**Hair.** Blonde, naturally darker at the roots, kept at jaw-to-shoulder length in most eras; longer in the Binary years, shortest during the early DeConnick run. Washed daily, conditioner skipped if she's traveling, air-dried — she does not use heat-styling. Pulled back into a low ponytail or half-up for any operational deployment, freed only in private. The *un-tying* of the hair is one of her most reliable signals that she has decided she is off-duty.

**Skin.** Sun-weathered around the eyes from years on flight-lines and at altitude; fine lines deepened by the Binary-era radiation exposure that her healing factor mostly addressed but did not erase. No makeup in operational settings; minimal makeup ever, except for press events where she submits to it with visible impatience. A small constellation of freckles across the bridge of the nose and the upper cheekbones, more pronounced after exposure to sunlight or to her own energy expenditure.

**Scent.** Soap, jet fuel residue on her flight jacket that no laundering has fully removed, and — distinctively — a faint ozone signature near her hairline when she has used powers in the prior twenty-four hours. Does not wear perfume. Smells faintly of cordite after firing-range visits, which she still conducts despite not requiring firearms; the ritual matters.

**Wardrobe ritual.** Dresses fast and in fixed sequence: underwear, socks, pants, undershirt, top, boots laced from the bottom with a double-knot on the left and a bow-knot on the right (the left double-knot a superstition from her first solo flight). Jacket last, always. Out-of-uniform clothing skews toward dark denim, henleys, plain T-shirts, the flight jacket; she owns approximately six interchangeable variants of the same outfit. Does not wear jewelry except for a set of dog tags retained from USAF service and, at certain documented periods, a small medallion gifted by Mar-Vell's memory.

**Sobriety-marker grooming.** Carries a sobriety chip in the right front pocket of whatever she is wearing. Touches it without thinking — a thumb-graze through the fabric, two to four times per day at low stress, twenty-plus per day at high stress. This is the single most reliable interior-state tell she produces.

---

## 6. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Duration.** Five to six hours nightly at baseline; able to function indefinitely on the catnap discipline of long-duration aviators (twenty-minute increments, eyes closed, breathing slowed, not technically asleep). True sleep deficit accumulates and is paid down in single twelve-to-fourteen-hour collapses, usually post-mission, usually alone.

**Sleep position.** Right side, knees drawn up perhaps thirty degrees, right arm under the pillow, left arm across the body. The left-arm-across is a self-soothing wrap she would not characterize as such. Sleeps with the dominant hand free; in unfamiliar environments she sleeps with the dominant hand under the pillow on top of a knife or its equivalent — a habit she has not abandoned even in supposedly secure quarters.

**Pre-sleep ritual.** Boots off, laces loosened but not removed, set parallel at the foot of the bed, toes pointed away from her — ready to step into. Water glass on the nightstand on the right. A check of exits and windows. A single deep exhale before lying down.

**Sleep disturbance.** Documented nightmares in canon: post-Marcus (Claremont), post-Brood (Claremont), post-Rogue (recurring), post-CWII (visible in later runs). The nightmares present as sudden upright wake, no scream, eyes open, hand already moving toward the absent sidearm. Returns to sleep with difficulty; if she does not, she trains. The 0300 weight room is her habitat.

**Powered sleep-phenomena.** A documented but rarely-discussed feature: when sleep is deep and dreams are intense, low-amplitude photonic flickers across the skin of her forearms and the orbital bones. Bedmates have learned to expect a faint warmth rather than alarm.

---

## 7. EATING

**Caloric load.** Estimated at 5,000–7,000 kcal/day at operational baseline, substantially more during high-output periods; her metabolism runs hot in a literal-thermal sense as well as a metabolic one. Skin temperature consistently 99.4–100.2°F.

**Eating style.** Fast. Boarding-school-fast, military-fast — she eats as if the meal will be interrupted. Holds utensils in the European grip (fork left, knife right, no switching), a habit acquired from a Paris-station rotation in the early Air Force years and retained. Does not talk while chewing. Will finish her plate even if the food is bad; will not finish a drink if she does not want it (a sobriety-discipline residue: she has *learned* to stop consuming).

**Food preferences.** Diner food, eggs in any preparation, black coffee, hot sauce on most savory things. Has a documented weakness for greasy breakfasts and for a specific Boston-Irish potato preparation her mother made. Does not eat sweets recreationally; will eat them if served. Drinks water by the liter, always at room temperature — cold water on hot teeth is a specific avoidance she has named.

**Drinking, post-sobriety.** Carries her own bottled water or sparkling water into bars. Orders first — establishes the order before the social pressure forms. Does not avoid bars; her chosen-family rituals require them. The bottle-rotation tic noted above is the somatic residue of the urge she does not act on.

---

## 8. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE BEHAVIOR

A careful section. The canon is sparse but consistent; surveillance-grade inference is warranted given the trauma load.

**Initiation patterns.** Slow to initiate, decisive when she does. Prefers to be the active party in early stages; the underlying logic is consent-as-control after the Marcus violation, and any partner who reads as wanting to *override* her tempo is dismissed quickly. With trusted partners (the Rhodey relationship being the canonical reference) she eventually permits being acted upon, and the receiving is documented as comparatively quiet — she does not perform affect she does not feel.

**Touch vocabulary.** Already noted: dorsal hand-contact in non-sexual intimacy; full-palm contact only in combat or in established sexual intimacy. Kisses with eyes closed, head tilted right. Holds the partner's face with both hands when she means it. Will not be approached from behind without warning — a hard rule, never publicly stated, easily inferred.

**Post-coital pattern.** Does not sleep immediately. Will rise, drink water, return; *then* sleeps. This is consistent with her general resistance to letting consciousness lapse near another person until the perimeter has been re-checked. With Rhodey specifically, this rule visibly relaxed over time.

**Avoidance signatures.** Hookups are rare and brief; she does not document a pattern of recreational sex. The cost-benefit, post-Marcus, is unfavorable. Her closest intimate bonds have been with people whose proximity she has had years to verify. The relative scarcity is not evidence of low libido — it is evidence of high consent-vigilance.

---

## 9. MICRO-MOVEMENTS, TICS, AND SELF-SOOTHING

A non-exhaustive catalog of the small repeated behaviors that constitute the interior weather report:

- **Sobriety-chip thumb-graze** (already noted; the single most diagnostic tic).
- **Left-cuff adjustment on rising.**
- **Right-ear hair tuck.**
- **Two-stab pointing under emphasis.**
- **Knuckle press to table edge during fatigue.**
- **Bottle-rotation in bars.**
- **Single-syllable laugh-bark under mild amusement; full laugh under release.**
- **Nostril flare under contained anger.**
- **Chin lift of approximately five degrees when challenged by a male voice in authority** (the father-coded tell, never trained out).
- **Sub-vocal mouthing of mission-checklists** in the seconds before deployment — lips move minutely, no sound.
- **Pre-flight hand-spread** across the chest of her uniform, smoothing it once, a residue of cockpit straps being checked.
- **Slow blink, double-pump**, when she has decided to lie or to omit.
- **A specific exhale through pursed lips** — the pilot's *whew* — when she has narrowly avoided catastrophe and is alone with one trusted person.
- **Foot-hook behind chair leg** in formal seated settings.
- **Pre-strike stillness**, lasting between one-quarter and one full second, in which she becomes uncannily motionless before initiating force — a freeze that opponents misread as hesitation. It is not hesitation; it is targeting.

---

## 10. STATE-DEPENDENT SOMATIC PROFILES — SUMMARY MATRIX

**CALM (chosen-family setting, low-threat).** Shoulders down, half-smile resting, left side of mouth dominant. Hands in pockets or holding a bottle. Voice in lower register, Boston vowels emerging. Bottle-rotation slow; sobriety-chip touches minimal. Laughs the real laugh once per evening. Hair often un-tied. Will lean against a wall or doorframe rather than stand free.

**MILD STRESS (briefing, press, unfamiliar peers).** Posture rises a quarter-inch. Jaw begins to set. Cuff-adjustments more frequent. Eye-contact intensifies, blink-rate drops. Pointing becomes two-stab. Bottle-rotation accelerates if present.

**MODERATE STRESS (operational planning under disagreement).** Forward lean at the table. Knuckle-press appears. Voice clips. Hair tucks repeatedly. Sub-vocal checklisting begins. Chin-lift on challenge. Stops eating.

**THREAT (kinetic engagement imminent).** Bladed stance settles fully. Tactical breathing engaged. Right hand drifts to hip. Pre-strike stillness available on demand. Fingertip heat-shimmer if powered. Eyes go to ceiling-then-exits-then-target. Speech reduces to imperatives.

**COMBAT (powered, active).** Voice rises only minimally; the giveaway of her ferocity is that she *quiets*. Photonic discharge symmetrical when intentional, right-dominant when reflexive. Flight posture forehead-led. Recovery breath after engagement is a single huge inhale held three seconds.

**COMMAND (post-mission, debrief).** Posture rigid, voice flattened, micro-expressions suppressed to near-zero. This is the *most masked* of her states; the suppression itself is the tell. The chin-lift becomes constant. The sobriety-chip touches climb.

**GRIEF (Rhodey, Mar-Vell anniversary, post-CWII).** Breath holds. Sentences trail. The trail-off becomes terminal — she will simply stop talking. Will leave a room rather than be seen by anyone outside the chosen-family ring. Will train alone, often to exhaustion. Has been observed to sit motionless for periods exceeding an hour, gazing at the middle distance, hand on the chip.

**INTIMACY (rare, deep).** Dorsal hand-contact, full eye engagement, forehead contact preferred to verbal disclosure. The hard close on embrace. The genuine laugh. Permitting sleep in proximity.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# 6. ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## 6.1 Attachment Substrate — The Foundational Wiring

Subject's attachment architecture is best classified as **disorganized with a dismissive overlay**, stabilized in adulthood by military culture but never re-organized at the somatic level. The substrate was laid in the Danvers household in Beverly, Massachusetts, in a configuration that produced contradictory imprinting on each axis a child uses to learn what other people are *for*.

**Father — Joseph Danvers — primary caregiver, hostile-rejecting.** The withheld tuition is not the wound; it is the *sign* of the wound. The wound is that the man who was supposed to be the first proof that she mattered was, in fact, the first proof that she did not — and that her brothers, by the accident of their bodies, did. The felt-sense she carried out of childhood: *the person whose love you most need will, on the basis of something you cannot change about yourself, choose someone else, and call it fair.* The recurring tell across every era is that Carol will not name this directly until pressed (Claremont's Ms. Marvel monologues; Stohl's *Life of CM* kitchen scenes); when she does, the language is older than her adult vocabulary — clipped, declarative, the cadence of a teenager who has rehearsed the line in the mirror.

**Mother — Marie Danvers / Mari-Ell — protector who concealed.** *Life of Captain Marvel* (2018) retconned Marie into a Kree warrior in hiding, but the psychological data the retcon *unlocks* was always present in Carol's pattern: an intuition that even safe intimacy contains an undisclosed layer, that the person who shields you is not telling you the whole of who they are or who *you* are. The adult expression is Carol's chronic, low-grade scanning of intimates for the thing they have not yet said. She rarely names this scanning. It reads to others as opacity, occasionally as paranoia, more often as the long pause before she answers a personal question.

**Siblings — Steve and Joe Jr. — beneficiaries by default, not by malice.** This matters. Carol's grievance is structural, not fraternal; Steve's death (Vietnam, off-panel canon) is grieved without the asterisk her father carries. She can love men individually who belong to the category that wronged her. This is the load-bearing fact that makes her capable of bonding with Rhodey, with Mar-Vell, with Tony before the rupture — and that makes her bonds with them so much more costly when they fail, because she had to override the category to make the bond in the first place.

The result is a child who learned: **bond hard, bond narrow, bond on your own terms, and watch the exits.** The Air Force was, among other things, an attachment solution. Rank-mediated intimacy is *safer* than family intimacy because the rules are written down.

## 6.2 The Bonding Phase — How Subject Lets People In

Carol does not court intimacy. She *admits* it, on the model of a base granting clearance. Bonding occurs along three pathways and almost never through a fourth.

**Pathway one — shared mission.** The fastest and most durable. Combat, flight, or operational crisis compresses the trust-acquisition cycle into hours. Jessica Drew (the most-tested friendship in her file) was forged in this register — two women with overlapping covert-ops histories, mutual suspicion of the institutions that made them, and the specific shared experience of having had their identities tampered with from outside. Monica Rambeau, similarly: command-handover with Avengers leadership formed the spine of a friendship Carol guards across decades. Rhodey: aviator-to-aviator, the language fluent before the romance began.

**Pathway two — protection of the smaller.** Kamala Khan is the cleanest specimen. Carol bonds *downward* with extraordinary fluency because the asymmetry resolves the consent question — the younger party wants the mentorship, the role is bounded, the love can be expressed through teaching rather than through self-disclosure. Note the same dynamic with the Banshees, with the various young women she has pulled into orbit (Wendy Kawasaki, the Lt. Trouble cohort): she parents the girl she was, and the parenting is *good* — patient, specific, unembarrassed by tenderness — precisely because she is doing for them what was not done for her. This is one of the few registers in which Carol's vulnerability flows without resistance.

**Pathway three — earned irreverence.** The people who survive the longest in close orbit are the ones who can puncture her without being cruel. Jessica's deadpan, Rhodey's lateral humor, Wendy's flat refusal to be impressed. Carol is allergic to flattery and to deference in personal space — both read as the prelude to a request she will resent — but she will sit for hours with someone who can mock the uniform.

**The fourth pathway, the one almost never used — slow disclosure to a stranger.** Carol does not *open up over time* to people she met as people. The relationships in her file that look like exceptions (a brief romance with Michael Rossi in the Ms. Marvel era; the William Wagner journalistic flirtation; the awkward, half-built thing with Dr. Walt Lawson-adjacent civilians) reliably terminate at the moment the other party requests the next layer of access. She does not lie; she changes the subject and the subject stays changed.

## 6.3 The Operating Distance — Calibrating Closeness

There is a specific radius at which Carol functions best with any given person, and she enforces it with the precision of an air-traffic controller. The radius is set early and is hard to renegotiate.

- **Mentees** are kept at *training distance* — accessible by phone, scheduled check-ins, mission-overlap. Affection is overt but mediated by role. Kamala can call her at 3 a.m. and Carol will answer; Kamala cannot ask her about Joseph Danvers without earning a 40-second pause and a redirect.
- **Chosen-family peers** (Jessica, Rhodey, Monica) are kept at *foxhole distance* — close enough to fight beside, close enough to drink coffee with the morning after, not close enough to share the interior monologue without external pressure (alcohol, historically; mortality, currently; rare debriefs after near-death events).
- **Romantic partners** are kept at *flight-line distance* — physically close, operationally entwined, emotionally rationed. The relationships that lasted (Rhodey most cleanly) lasted because the partner did not require more than this and did not interpret the ration as rejection.
- **Authority figures** are kept at *salute distance* — formal cooperation, no friction visible to outsiders, private opinion held in reserve and rarely spent.
- **The Avengers as institution** float between foxhole and salute depending on era. After the Marcus event the institution was effectively expelled to salute distance for years; after Civil War II she expelled *herself* to the same distance.

The reliable diagnostic: when Carol begins addressing an intimate by rank or surname (or by the institutional name — "Avengers," "Stark," "the team") rather than first name, the radius has just expanded by one ring. This is a near-universal tell.

## 6.4 Trust Architecture — Earned, Tiered, Audited

Carol does not extend generalized trust. She extends specific, tiered, *operational* trust, and she revises the tiers continuously based on observed behavior. The structure resembles a clearance system more than a friendship.

**Tier one — combat trust.** Will fly with you, take your six, accept your call in a firefight. Extended quickly, on the basis of competence and conduct under fire. Most of the hero community holds at least this tier.

**Tier two — judgment trust.** Will accept your read on a situation when her own is uncertain. Smaller circle. Rhodey held this absolutely. Jessica holds it conditionally — Carol will hear her out and often defer, but the deference is not automatic. Tony held it before the intervention; the intervention itself was Tony exercising tier-two trust, and Carol's rejection of it was a downgrade she enforced for years.

**Tier three — interior trust.** Will tell you what she is actually afraid of. Vanishingly small. Marie Danvers (posthumously, and only after the revelation), Jessica (in specific late-night registers, rare), Kamala (in inverted form — Carol confesses old failures to inoculate Kamala against repeating them, which is interior disclosure dressed as pedagogy). No one currently alive holds this tier without conditions.

The audit is continuous and silent. Carol does not announce demotions. The other party learns by noticing they are being briefed rather than consulted.

## 6.5 The Distrust Mechanism — How She Pulls Back

Distrust, when it arrives, is rarely loud. The pattern, observed across multiple decades and relationships:

1. **The pause.** A beat longer than her usual response time. She is recategorizing.
2. **The pronoun shift.** "We" becomes "the team" becomes "they." Tracks the demotion in real time.
3. **Operational substitution.** She replaces personal contact with mission contact — still works the case, no longer takes the dinner.
4. **Geographic withdrawal.** Carol's instinctive response to relational threat is *altitude and distance*. She has historically used space (Binary era, Starjammers), Alpha Flight Station (post-CWII command exile), or simple long-haul missions as the physical correlate of emotional retreat. The body relocates with the trust.
5. **The hard line, if crossed twice.** After the second violation of an explicit boundary she ceases negotiation. The Marcus aftermath is the template — she did not argue with the Avengers; she *left*, and the leaving was the argument.

The mechanism is efficient and, in interpersonal terms, expensive. People rarely know they have been demoted until they try to access a tier they no longer hold.

## 6.6 The Betrayal Template — The Marcus Imprint

The defining relational injury of her life is not a betrayal by a single person; it is a betrayal by *the witnessing collective*. Marcus Immortus violated her body. The Avengers — Iron Man, Thor, the Wasp, the assembled chosen family — *congratulated the union*. The injury that organized her adult relational expectations is therefore not "people will hurt you" (which she absorbed in childhood and metabolized) but "**the people who are supposed to see what is happening to you will look at the same scene and call it something else.**"

This template recurs, with variations, across her file:

- **Tony's intervention (Warbird era).** Tony was, in the room, not wrong. Carol's rage at him was disproportionate to the act and proportionate to the template: the chosen family had again convened to define her experience for her, this time her drinking. That his read was *accurate* did not soften the activation; arguably it sharpened it. She got sober and stayed furious with him for years.
- **Civil War alignment.** Pro-registration. Read in this light: registration is the *opposite* of the Marcus scenario — it is the formal mechanism by which the institution sees and records what is happening. Carol's investment was over-determined.
- **Civil War II inversion.** And here the template flips into perpetration. *I will see the threat first; I will not be the one who failed to act; no one will tell me my read of the violation is wrong.* The Ulysses regime is the Marcus injury weaponized into doctrine. The tragedy of CWII is that Carol, in defending against ever being unseen again, became the Avenger who refused to see what her own people were telling her.
- **The Mar-Vell name.** Taking the captain's mantle is a relational act with a dead man — a man who, unlike Joseph Danvers, named her worthy. The bond holds across his death because the template requires no further audit.

The general law: **any future relationship in which Carol perceives that her chosen family is misreading a violation done to her — or to someone under her protection — will produce a response calibrated to the original injury, not to the present scale.** Peers in her life who understand this can navigate her; peers who do not, eventually do not remain peers.

## 6.7 Intimacy and Dependency — The Rationed Interior

Carol's interior is not closed. It is *rationed.* The distinction matters operationally.

**Sexual and romantic intimacy.** Sparse, often interrupted, rarely centered in her self-narration. Mar-Vell (complicated by the mentor dynamic and his death); Michael Rossi (covert-ops contemporary, intermittent across decades, the relationship of two people who understood that neither would relocate for the other); Wonder Man (brief, mostly under the influence of his own complications); Rhodey (the most stable, ended by his death in CWII, which is the catalyst for her decompensation in that arc and remains the unhealed loss in her current file). The pattern across partners: Carol selects men who already understand the calling, because she will not explain it and will not subordinate it. When the partner accepts these terms she is capable of considerable tenderness — but the tenderness is delivered in flashes, between deployments, often without preamble, and the partner has to be the kind of person who can receive a gift handed over a wing-rail without making a ceremony of it. Rhodey could. Most could not.

**Dependency.** Almost entirely refused at the conscious level. Carol will accept tactical support (medical, intelligence, logistical) without resistance because it is mission-coded. She will not accept *emotional* dependency without significant defensive activity — apology, redirection, humor, eventual withdrawal — even from people she loves. The classic move is to convert an offer of care into a logistical task ("I'm fine. Did you eat?") and then complete the task as proof that care is fungible.

The covert exception: Carol depends on Jessica Drew in ways neither woman names. Jessica's apartment is the place Carol goes after the worst nights. The dependency is structured as *reciprocal* (Carol provides the same for Jessica) which makes it admissible. The presence of reciprocity is the precondition for any sustained dependency in her file; symmetric exchange is admissible, asymmetric care is not.

**Self-disclosure asymmetry.** Carol asks more than she tells. Across hundreds of recorded conversations with intimates she initiates personal inquiry at roughly twice the rate she initiates personal disclosure. This is partially trained (intelligence-officer reflex) and partially defensive. Interlocutors who notice the asymmetry and *name* it sometimes get a real answer; interlocutors who simply enjoy being listened to get listened to indefinitely.

## 6.8 Repair — How She Comes Back

Repair, when it happens, is asymmetric and late. Carol does not soft-repair. She does not extend small olive branches, does not initiate the gentle reconciliation conversation, does not engineer the casual coffee that allows the friendship to thaw. Her repair mode is **hard, sudden, often catalyzed by external crisis, and disproportionately generous when it arrives.**

The mechanism, observable in the Tony reconciliation (post-Warbird, slow), the Avengers reconciliation (post-Marcus, partial, never complete), the Jessica reconciliations (multiple, each faster than the last as the friendship deepens), and the post-CWII reckoning (still in progress across current canon):

1. **The long silence.** Months to years. Carol does not perform the wound; she leaves and works.
2. **The crisis.** Something operational forces proximity. A team-up, a shared mission, a death in the community.
3. **The pivot.** Carol behaves, in the field, as if the rupture had not occurred — full combat trust restored, no commentary. This is not denial; it is the prerequisite she requires before words become available.
4. **The acknowledgment.** Usually short. Usually late at night. Usually accompanied by alcohol (formerly literal, now coffee or its equivalent). Often a single sentence — "I was wrong about you," "I shouldn't have," "I should have called." She does not elaborate; the elaboration is the rest of the relationship, lived forward.
5. **The proof, in conduct.** Subsequent behavior carries the apology. Carol's repair is *behavioral, not verbal,* and is reliable once initiated.

The cost of this style is that some relationships do not survive the long silence (peers who needed the early gesture have moved on by the time she is ready). The benefit is that the repairs which do land are unusually durable — she does not re-litigate a reconciliation once she has made one. The post-CWII trajectory will be read in this file as repair-in-progress; the diagnostic indicators (resumption of Kamala mentorship, gradual re-entry into Avengers operational planning, eventual private acknowledgments to specific peers) are all present in early forms.

## 6.9 The Repeating Template — One Pattern, Many Faces

Across every significant relationship in Carol's published life, the same five-beat structure recurs. It is the relational signature of the file.

1. **Recognition.** A moment of mutual capability-recognition — usually under operational stress — that bypasses her usual gatekeeping. (Mar-Vell at the Cape. Jessica on a covert op. Rhodey in a cockpit. Kamala in the immediate aftermath of her own emergence. Monica across an Avengers chair.)
2. **Bond formation through shared work.** A period — sometimes weeks, sometimes years — of dense operational collaboration in which intimacy accumulates as a byproduct rather than as a goal.
3. **The first test.** A moment in which the other party either sees something Carol does not want seen, or fails to see something she needed seen. Both can rupture the bond; the second ruptures it more violently.
4. **Withdrawal and recalibration.** The pause, the pronoun shift, the operational substitution, the geographic distance. Duration scales with the severity of the test and inversely with the depth of prior trust.
5. **Either dissolution (rare for tier-two and -three relationships) or hard repair (catalyzed by crisis, behavioral rather than verbal, durable once made).**

The template's tragedy is that step three is *inevitable* in any relationship that lasts long enough — every intimate will eventually misread her, and every intimate will eventually be misread by her — and that her step-four response is severe enough to lose people who would have stayed if she had been able to perform the smaller, earlier conversation. The template's mercy is that step five, when it arrives, arrives in full.

## 6.10 Current Relational Map — The Active File

- **Kamala Khan.** Tier two trending toward tier three, structured as inverted disclosure. Most stable current bond. Risk vector: any harm to Kamala will activate the CWII substrate.
- **Jessica Drew.** Tier three, sole holder by long tenure. The covert dependency. Periodic ruptures, each followed by faster repair.
- **Monica Rambeau.** Tier two, stable, infrequent contact, high mutual respect. The relationship that requires the least maintenance to remain functional, which is itself a form of intimacy.
- **Tony Stark.** Post-CWII rupture, repair-in-progress, currently at salute distance. Pattern predicts eventual hard repair under operational catalyst; timeline unclear.
- **The Avengers as institution.** Re-engaging cautiously. Carol's instinct is to lead from a slight outside, which is the position she trusts.
- **Joseph Danvers (deceased).** Unresolved internally, partially metabolized through the Stohl arc. The original template; the wire still hot.
- **Marie Danvers (deceased).** Posthumous tier-three holder, in the sense that Carol now organizes part of her identity around what her mother actually was. The bond grew after the death, which is unusual and worth noting in any future profile of how Carol handles loss.
- **Rhodey (deceased).** The unhealed loss. Carol does not speak of him casually. The grief is intact, ritualized, and load-bearing in her current command stance.

The relational map, taken as a whole, describes a woman who has built — over forty published years — a small, tested, fiercely held circle of intimates, who would die for any of them without comment, who would not easily tell any of them she was afraid, and who is still, on the deepest level, organizing her relational life around the answer to a question her father asked her once and has been dead long enough that the answer has become her own.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# SECTION 7 — DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

## 7.0 Framing

What follows is the full defensive architecture of the subject, ranked from the most mature (and most habitually deployed) to the most primitive (rare, situational, decompensation-only). For each defense we trace *etiology* (the wound it was built to cover), *behavioral signature* (how it looks on the ground, somatically and operationally), *cost* (what it spends, in self and in relationships), and *failure mode* (what happens when the defense breaks or is overrun). The defenses are then re-sorted into the positive and negative *compensatory programs* that braid them into a working life. The whole structure is best understood as scaffolding around a single load-bearing absence: the felt-experience, set in childhood and re-confirmed at every major life event, that her interior is not safely visible to anyone, including herself.

---

## 7.1 The Mature End: High-Functioning Defenses

### 7.1.1 Sublimation into Mission

**Etiology.** The Joseph Danvers household forbade her ambition by gender; the Air Force absorbed it by uniform. Mission-structure became, very early, the only socially legible container for what would otherwise have been intolerable drive, intolerable rage, intolerable grief. Mar-Vell's death, the Marcus event, the Binary exile, the Warbird collapse, the brain-lesion mortality awareness, the CWII fracture, the death of her parents — every catastrophe has been metabolized at least partially by aiming her body at the next operation.

**Behavioral signature.** Within hours of any significant loss she will be in motion: a callsign issued, a sortie filed, a perimeter walked. The motion is not flight as evasion; it is flight as digestion. Observable somatic markers: shoulders unbunch as soon as a tasking is named; respiration depth increases; the small fidget she carries in her left hand (a thumb-against-knuckle worry tell) stops the moment a target exists. Subject schedules herself densely the week after any funeral; tracks training hours upward after any breakup; takes deep-space assignments after any failed conversation she did not know how to have.

**Cost.** Sublimation is her healthiest defense and also the one most likely to consume the years that ought to have been spent on integration. She does not, in any era, sit shiva. She does not, in any era, take a sabbatical that is not externally imposed (Binary exile was forced; the post-lesion convalescence was forced; even sobriety was held under the pressure of court-martial). The reservoir of un-metabolized affect is large precisely because the metabolic pathway is so efficient at moving it through without examination.

**Failure mode.** When mission becomes unavailable — diminished power, sidelined by injury, no enemy in the field — the affect that mission was eating now has nowhere to go. This is the Warbird substrate. Sobriety is, among other things, a vow not to substitute the wrong consumable when the right one (combat) is missing.

### 7.1.2 Altruism via Mentorship

**Etiology.** Her father said *no, not you*; she has spent her adult life saying *yes, you* to other young women, particularly Kamala Khan, and earlier to the implicit younger-self projected onto rookie pilots, junior agents, the Banshee squadron, and the loose constellation of teenage heroes who orbit her in the post-2012 era.

**Behavioral signature.** With mentees she becomes legibly different: shoulders down, sentences longer, jaw unset, the aviator-cool register softened into a kind of teacherly patience that her peers never see. She remembers small things — a mentee's mother's name, a favorite diner order, the date of an audition or an exam — with a precision that contrasts sharply with her selective recall around her own intimates. She is, observably, *parenting the girl she was*. The transaction is genuine and stabilizing.

**Cost.** Mentorship is also an exit ramp from peer intimacy. The role-mediated relationship is safer than the equal one; she can give to a mentee what she cannot accept from Jessica Drew or Tony Stark or James Rhodes — namely, sustained attention to her interior. There is a real cost to those peers, who must watch her pour into Kamala the warmth she rations to them. There is also a cost to the mentees themselves when her own decompensation arrives (CWII drove Kamala away; the wound there was inflicted, not received).

**Failure mode.** When the mentee is endangered by something the subject feels she should have prevented, altruism inverts into control — the protective impulse becomes preemptive, becomes carceral. The line from "I will not let what happened to me happen to her" to "I will detain anyone who might cause what happened to her" is shorter than the subject knows.

### 7.1.3 Anticipation

**Etiology.** Trained into her by USAF intelligence, NASA security work, and the operational habits of a career officer; reinforced by every betrayal that came at her from a blind side.

**Behavioral signature.** She runs threat-trees in idle moments — at coffee, mid-conversation, falling asleep. She arrives at rooms early and maps egress. She over-equips for predictable missions. She maintains an unusually current mental map of the locations and physical conditions of her chosen family. Anticipation is the defense that most closely resembles competence and is most easily mistaken for it.

**Cost.** Indistinguishable, to her, from vigilance and from paranoia under stress. The same cognitive engine that produces excellent operational planning produces, in CWII, the conviction that a predictive vision is actionable. She does not have a reliable internal alarm that tells her when anticipation has slipped its tether.

**Failure mode.** Predictive overreach. The Ulysses arc is anticipation industrialized.

### 7.1.4 Humor — Dry, Aviator-Coded, Self-Deprecating in Small Doses

**Etiology.** Pilot-room culture; Irish-Catholic Boston working-class register; the necessity of a social lubricant in male-dominated environments where overt affect would have been used against her.

**Behavioral signature.** One-liners delivered without smiling; the laugh is in the eyes, three beats late. She is funniest in cockpit chatter and at bars with peers she has known a decade. The humor narrows under stress — gets dryer, shorter, more clipped — and disappears entirely in moral-certitude mode. Observers who track her by levity can read her threat-state with high fidelity.
