**Cost.** Low. This is one of her cleanest defenses. The only tax it pays is that intimates who confuse the dryness for distance sometimes give up too early on the conversation that would have followed.

### 7.1.5 Suppression (the Conscious Kind)

**Etiology.** Officer training; the explicit doctrine of *mission first, feelings after action review*. Critically distinct from repression: she *knows* what she is setting aside and *intends* to come back to it.

**Behavioral signature.** Visible micro-pause before re-engaging a tactical problem after an emotional intrusion — a half-second where the face resets. End-of-day journaling, intermittently practiced, is her attempt to honor the return. Sobriety meetings, during the early years, functioned similarly.

**Cost.** She is good at the setting-aside and inconsistent at the returning. Items get filed and not opened. The lesion-arc memory loss accelerated this, since material she had postponed for later examination was, in some cases, materially gone.

**Failure mode.** Pure repression. When the load exceeds the conscious manager, items move below the line and start steering behavior unannounced.

---

## 7.2 The Neurotic Middle: The Workhorse Defenses

### 7.2.1 Reaction Formation Against Vulnerability

**Etiology.** Every time she has shown softness — to her father, to the Avengers in the wake of the Marcus event, to Tony at the intervention, to herself in the bottle — the response has been weaponized, ignored, or punitive. She learned to invert.

**Behavioral signature.** The clearest tell in the entire file. The more frightened or grieving she is, the more declarative her speech becomes; the further her body tilts forward; the harder her jaw sets; the more her vocabulary contracts to the imperative mood. "Higher, further, faster" is, read clinically, an inverted prayer — the slogan you adopt precisely because *lower, closer, slower* is what you cannot bear to be. After Rhodey's death she does not weep on-panel; she expands operational tempo. After the brain-lesion diagnosis she does not seek counsel; she schedules the mission.

**Cost.** Enormous, sustained, and largely paid in relationships. The people who love her experience her grief-state as her authority-state and back off from comforting her precisely when she most needs it. The defense thus reproduces the original injury — *no one sees what is actually happening to me* — and confirms its necessity.

**Failure mode.** Decompensation into authoritarianism. When the affect under the inversion is large enough, the declarativeness scales into ideology. CWII is reaction formation at command altitude.

### 7.2.2 Intellectualization / Tactical Reframing

**Etiology.** Pilot-officer culture; her own high-g cognitive style; the discovery, sometime in the Warbird-to-sobriety transition, that personal pain *named as a tactical problem* becomes survivable.

**Behavioral signature.** Emotional content is consistently translated into operational variables — relationships become "comms," grief becomes "load," her own fear becomes "noise," another person's fear becomes a "vector." She runs after-action reviews on conversations with her therapist as if they were sorties. She has, more than once, drawn a literal whiteboard about a friendship.

**Cost.** Real intimacy requires a register she has trained herself out of. Partners and peers who can speak fluent tactics get the most of her; the rest get the shape of her, well-rendered, missing the center.

**Failure mode.** When the problem genuinely is not tactical — when somebody just needs her to *be sad with them* — she defaults to fixing, and the relationship logs another small failure.

### 7.2.3 Identification with the Aggressor

**Etiology.** Joseph Danvers controlled her by gendered prohibition; she escaped him into a structure (the USAF) that controls everyone by uniform. The structure, being legible and rule-bound, felt safer than the household. She has, ever since, trusted structures that resemble her father in form while differing in content — hierarchical, demanding, ostensibly meritocratic.

**Behavioral signature.** She supports registration. She accepts command roles she does not enjoy. She defaults, under stress, to escalating authority rather than horizontal consensus. She finds Steve Rogers easier to argue with than Jessica Drew, because Steve is a structure and Jessica is a person. When she catches the trait in herself — and she does, increasingly, in the post-Stohl era — she works against it visibly, particularly in mentorship of Kamala, where she is deliberate about *not* reproducing the prohibitive paternal voice.

**Cost.** This is the defense most likely, over a long career, to put her on the wrong side of the people who love her. Identification with the aggressor is what makes the CWII detentions feel, from the inside, like duty.

**Failure mode.** She becomes, momentarily, the thing she escaped. The post-CWII self-assessment — that she was wrong — is a victory of insight against this defense, not the absence of the defense.

### 7.2.4 Displacement

**Etiology.** Mostly directed outward from unmetabolized rage at her father, at the Avengers-circa-#200, at the Brood, at Rogue, at Tony.

**Behavioral signature.** Sub-acute and largely contained, but observable: the intensity she brings to certain villains is disproportionate to their tactical importance — particularly anything coded as a violator of bodily autonomy, anything coded as a paternal authority demanding her compliance, anything coded as a thief of self. Cockpit kills run cleaner than ground engagements; she is more efficient against the impersonal.

**Cost.** Occasional collateral. Allies in the wrong proximity to a displacement-rich engagement have, more than once, found themselves on the receiving end of a snap she would not have delivered cold.

### 7.2.5 Undoing

**Etiology.** Sober-recovery practice; survivor-guilt around Mar-Vell and Rhodey; the unfinished business with the Avengers post-#200.

**Behavioral signature.** Small ritualized acts of repair, frequently disproportionate to the original injury. After harsh words she will, hours later, drop off coffee, fix something in the recipient's apartment, run an unprompted training session for their team. After CWII she takes on missions specifically calculated to repay debts to those she alienated. The undoing is sincere and partial — sincere because she means it, partial because she will not, in the same gesture, name what she is repairing.

**Cost.** Unnamed repair is a half-repair. The recipients know what the coffee is for, and resent slightly that the coffee is the only language available.

### 7.2.6 Rationalization

**Etiology.** Defense of a self-image that cannot afford to be wrong about the big things.

**Behavioral signature.** Post-hoc operational justifications for decisions made affectively. CWII produced extensive rationalization architecture before it produced the admission of error. She is, however, capable of demolishing her own rationalizations when shown the contrary evidence by someone she trusts — a feature that distinguishes her from genuinely characterological denial.

---

## 7.3 The Lower Neurotic Floor: Defenses That Show Under Strain

### 7.3.1 Isolation of Affect

**Etiology.** Combat necessity; the Warbird crash taught her, paradoxically, that feeling-while-flying is dangerous. She over-corrected.

**Behavioral signature.** She can describe traumatic content — the Marcus event, the Brood, Rhodey's death — in flat, clinical sentences. The affect is not gone; it is fenced from the verbal channel. Observers who only listen will mistake the fence for resolution. Observers who watch the body (the breath-catch before the Marcus name; the millisecond of flinch at "Rhodey") see otherwise.

**Cost.** Therapists, partners, and biographers receive a narrative that they wrongly take as worked-through.

### 7.3.2 Avoidance Routed Through Geography

**Etiology.** Boston is hard. The Cape is hard. Specific rooms are hard.

**Behavioral signature.** Deep-space assignments, by her own pattern, cluster around emotionally untenable Earth-side situations. The Binary exile was forced by depowering; the subsequent decades of intermittent off-world deployment were, more often than not, chosen. She does not say *I am leaving because I cannot stand this*; she says *I am needed out there*. Both are true. The order of operations is what matters.

**Cost.** Earthbound relationships starve in increments.

### 7.3.3 Counter-Dependence

**Etiology.** The intervention. The Marcus applause. Every offer of help that turned out to be a leash.

**Behavioral signature.** Reflexive *I'm fine* before the question is finished. Door closed when convalescing. Will not ask for the favor that costs nothing. Will accept the favor only if she has already framed the return obligation. The depth of this defense is best measured by how rarely it cracks: across the entire published life, the moments she has genuinely *let someone in* without simultaneously managing the transaction can be counted on one hand.

**Cost.** Loneliness, self-imposed and constantly under-reported.

---

## 7.4 The Primitive End: Decompensation-Only Defenses

These are not baseline. They appear only at high stress, and their appearance is itself diagnostic of system overload.

### 7.4.1 Splitting

**Surfaces:** CWII at full operational scale; smaller versions visible during Live Kree or Dead and immediately post-intervention with Tony.

**Mechanism.** Under sustained threat to her decisional authority, the social field bifurcates: those who agree are allies-in-full, those who dissent are obstacles-in-full. Nuance collapses. The capacity to hold a friend as simultaneously dear and wrong — present in her healthy baseline — disappears.

**Tell.** Pronoun shift from "we" to "I" in operational speech, sometimes within the same sentence. Friends become surnames; surnames become categories.

### 7.4.2 Acting Out — Historically via Alcohol

**Surfaces:** Warbird era, fully resolved on the substance axis; the underlying impulse — to discharge unbearable affect through behavior — remains and now finds other vehicles (overreach, over-deployment, the deep-space exit).

**Note.** Sobriety did not remove the impulse; it removed one route. The architecture above is, in part, the system of dams built where the bottle used to be.

### 7.4.3 Dissociation — Historical, Mostly Integrated

**Surfaces:** The original Ms. Marvel emergence, with amnestic gaps. Residue visible in her continued self-bifurcation language ("Carol" versus "Captain Marvel") and in micro-fugue moments under acute trauma (post-Marcus, post-Rogue). Largely resolved; flagged for clinical awareness because the substrate exists and could re-emerge under sufficient load.

### 7.4.4 Omnipotent Control — Power-Mediated

**Mechanism.** When the defenses above are saturated, the existence of cosmic-tier power offers a defense unavailable to ordinary subjects: *make the world conform*. She does not often reach for this; the discipline against it is one of her most genuine moral achievements. But the capacity exists, and the CWII detentions are its early-warning shape — not omnipotent control in full, but the same hand reaching.

---

## 7.5 The Positive Compensatory Program

Braided from the mature defenses above, the following stabilizing structures are observable across decades:

- **Aviator-culture ritual.** Flight jackets, callsigns, the Banshee bar, the specific cadence of pre-flight checks performed even when unnecessary. These are containing rituals that locate her in a self she chose.
- **Mentorship architecture.** Kamala is the cleanest example; the broader pattern includes Monica Rambeau (peer-mentor, reciprocal), the rotating cast of younger pilots and heroes, and the more diffuse role she plays as a legible woman-in-command for the next generation. The mentorship is real care and also a corrective rewriting of her own girlhood.
- **Sobriety practice.** The discipline itself, the meetings (intermittent), the inventory habit, the relapse-vigilance. Generalizes — usefully — into emotional self-monitoring she would otherwise not perform.
- **Chosen family, narrow and deep.** Jessica Drew across decades; Rhodey while he lived; Monica; Kamala; a handful of others. The narrowness is the price; the depth is the gain.
- **Matrilineal integration (post-Stohl).** Active claiming of the Kree/Marie lineage as a counterweight to the Joseph-coded paternal structure. The integration is incomplete but ongoing, and the direction is correct.
- **Service to the weaker.** Genuine, sustained, costly, and self-stabilizing. The defense most indistinguishable from virtue, because in her case it is largely both.

---

## 7.6 The Negative Compensatory Program

The same engine, run in the other direction:

- **Control-as-safety.** When outcome cannot be controlled, access is — to her interior, to information, to operational latitude. The detention regime is the public-policy form; the closed door at home is the private one.
- **Behavioral rigidity downstream of sobriety discipline.** All-or-nothing framing generalizes. *I do not drink* becomes *I do not waver* becomes *I do not stand down*.
- **Mission as anesthesia.** Sublimation in its overused form. The next operation is always available; the un-grieved item is always postponable.
- **Counter-dependence as identity.** *I do this alone* is, by now, partly load-bearing for her self-concept. Asking for help would require dismantling not just a habit but a definition.
- **Authority-trust under stress.** Identification with the aggressor in its political form. Structures resembling the paternal one feel safer than the horizontal alternatives, particularly when she is frightened.
- **Geographic exit.** Deep space as the elegant displacement. The cosmos is, among other things, a long way from the conversation she did not have.

---

## 7.7 Rank-Order Summary (Most to Least Habitually Deployed)

1. **Sublimation into mission** — daily, structural.
2. **Suppression** — daily, conscious.
3. **Anticipation** — daily, trained.
4. **Reaction formation against vulnerability** — situational, near-automatic under grief or fear.
5. **Humor** — daily baseline, narrows under stress.
6. **Intellectualization / tactical reframing** — high-frequency, especially in interpersonal load.
7. **Altruism via mentorship** — sustained, role-specific.
8. **Identification with the aggressor** — chronic, partially in-awareness.
9. **Counter-dependence** — chronic, ego-syntonic.
10. **Isolation of affect** — moderate stress.
11. **Displacement** — moderate stress, combat-channeled.
12. **Undoing** — post-conflict, ritualized.
13. **Rationalization** — situational, especially around contested decisions.
14. **Avoidance via geography** — episodic, major decisions.
15. **Splitting** — decompensation only.
16. **Acting out (historically: alcohol)** — fully suppressed; substrate persists.
17. **Dissociation** — historical, largely integrated, monitored.
18. **Omnipotent control** — capacity present, deployment disciplined against.

---

## 7.8 Closing Observation for the Section

The defensive architecture above is, taken whole, the architecture of a competent person who has not been allowed to be soft and has therefore built a hard exterior with surprisingly sophisticated internal plumbing. The plumbing is what saves her — the mature defenses are real, the integration work is real, the sobriety is real, the mentorship is real. The hard exterior is what endangers her, and others, when the plumbing is overloaded. The single most reliable predictor of overreach in this subject is not the magnitude of the external threat but the magnitude of the *internal* affect she is currently refusing to name. When she is grieving, watch the orders she gives. When she is frightened, watch the doors she closes. When she is unseen, watch the altitude.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: DANVERS, CAROL SUSAN JANE
## Section: Longitudinal Psychological Profile

*Methodological note. What follows tracks the subject's clinical picture across roughly five operational decades of published existence, partitioned not by calendar but by phase-change in her own functioning. Each phase is described under three rails — affect regulation, cognitive style, self-concept — followed by the proximate stressors and the structural carry-over into the next phase. Frameworks invoked: Bowlby/Main on attachment; Vaillant's hierarchy of defenses; Linehan on affect-dysregulation in trauma; Herman on complex PTSD's three-stage course; Janoff-Bulman on shattered assumptions; van der Kolk on somatic encoding; Kernberg on identity-diffusion; the obsessive-compulsive personality literature (Shapiro, *Neurotic Styles*) for the trait-scaffolding that recurs at every stage.*

---

### Phase I — Pre-Origin (childhood through Air Force / NASA service)

**Affect regulation.** The household teaches her, early, that the affect of a daughter is contraband. Joseph Danvers' withholding of tuition is not an isolated decision; it is a chronic communicative environment in which Carol's wanting is met with negation. The adaptation is classically *over-controlled*: a child whose emotional displays will be punished or ignored learns to compress affect into action. By enlistment age, she has rehearsed a regulatory style in which feeling is converted to doing — anger to discipline, grief to competence, fear to drill. The Boston working-class Catholic frame supplies the moral vocabulary (duty, endurance, suffering as proof) that makes this conversion feel virtuous rather than effortful.

**Cognitive style.** Fast, concrete, kinesthetic, externally-oriented. There is no published evidence of an introspective adolescent journal-keeper; she chooses aviation, intelligence work, and physical mastery. The cognitive signature that will persist for sixty years is *pattern-recognition under time pressure with action-bias* — exactly the cognition the USAF will reward and refine. Ambiguity is metabolized by motion. The shadow of this style is already visible: she will not be the officer who calls the meeting; she will be the officer who calls the strike.

**Self-concept.** Negatively-defined and oppositional. She knows what she is not (small, contained, *not you*) more vividly than what she is. The earliest stable self-image is *the one who is not stopped*. This is identity built by refusal rather than affirmation — durable, but brittle in the specific way refusal-identities always are: it requires an antagonist to feel real. Her mother's concealed Kree nature, learned only decades later but present in the household as an emotional weather pattern, contributes a felt-sense that intimate truth is partial — a substrate finding that will fund a lifetime of difficulty trusting her own perceptions of relational warmth.

**Defensive structure (Vaillantian).** Heavily *sublimative* (the healthiest neurotic defense), with reaction-formation against weakness and incipient intellectualization. No regressive or psychotic-tier defenses observable.

---

### Phase II — Psyche-Magnitron and the Dissociative Ms. Marvel Years (late 1960s onset; 1977–1980 published)

**Affect regulation.** Catastrophic insult to a system that had achieved high-functional over-control. The Psyche-Magnitron event is a bodily violation she cannot narrate (she has no memory of it as power-acquisition) layered onto a body she had previously mastered through training. The system's response is the most extreme regulatory move available short of psychosis: *splitting consciousness itself*. The Ms. Marvel persona carries the affect, the power, the agency the Carol persona is not permitted to feel; the Carol persona carries the continuity of a workable civilian life. There are amnestic seams. Affect is not so much regulated as *quarantined*.

**Cognitive style.** Bifurcated. Carol-mode: investigative, journalistic (the *Woman* magazine job is a relevant cognitive habitat — observe, frame, publish), competent but increasingly puzzled by her own time-loss. Ms.-Marvel-mode: tactical, declarative, untroubled. Critically, neither persona is fully accessing the other's data — the cardinal cognitive feature of a dissociative presentation. The "seventh sense" — a brief precognitive flicker — is best read clinically as the cross-membrane *leak* between the two systems, the part of her that knows what the other part is about to do.

**Self-concept.** Identity-diffusion in the Kernbergian sense, organized around two pseudo-stable poles. She cannot integrate the powered self into the autobiographical self because she has no narrative of acquiring it; powers without origin-memory feel like possession, not capability. The published behavior — disorientation, partial memory, alternating presentation — meets historical criteria for a dissociative identity organization, etiologically coherent with developmental invalidation plus acute somatic violation.

**Defensive structure.** *Dissociation* ascends to primary defense, with sublimation continuing in both modes (Carol writes; Ms. Marvel fights). This is the only phase of her life in which her defensive structure crosses into the *immature* tier in Vaillant's hierarchy. It will not recur in this form, but the *seam* it leaves — the bifurcated self-talk of "Carol" versus "Captain Marvel" — persists for the rest of her published existence as a residue.

---

### Phase III — The Marcus Atrocity and Its Immediate Aftermath (1980–1981)

**Affect regulation.** Total collapse of the regulatory architecture, masked by a scripted-affect surface (the original *Avengers* #200 panels). What the text initially depicts as resolution is, read clinically, a peritraumatic dissociative response: flat affect, compliance, the language of others put in her mouth. Claremont's corrective in *Avengers Annual* #10 is the moment the *actual* affect arrives — and it arrives as rage, the only register her over-controlled system has ever permitted as an outlet. The episode establishes the affective template that will dominate the next four decades: when the regulatory dam fails, what comes through is not sadness, not fear, but *incandescent moral fury*, and the targets are the people who failed to see.

**Cognitive style.** Janoff-Bulman's three core assumptions — benevolence of the world, meaningfulness of events, worthiness of self — are not merely shaken but inverted in a single arc. The cognitive consequence is a permanent recalibration: she will, henceforward, run threat-assessment on her own allies as a background process. This is not paranoia; it is updated Bayesian priors based on direct evidence that the people closest to her can fail to perceive her violation in real time.

**Self-concept.** The Marcus event creates the deepest wire in the entire personality structure: *bodily autonomy + unseen-by-witnesses*. The self-concept reorganizes around the necessity of being the one who *names* what is happening. She will, from this point on, struggle to allow anyone else to frame her experience for her — a trait that reads as strength in command settings and as brittleness in intimate ones.

**Defensive structure.** Sublimation re-ascends, but now coupled with a new defense that will become signature: *moral reframing under threat* — the conversion of personal injury into ethical principle, articulable in public, defensible in tribunal. Healthy in moderation; the engine of CWII-grade overreach when uncoupled from peer correction.

---

### Phase IV — Binary and Self-Exile (early-to-mid 1980s)

**Affect regulation.** Geographic solution to an affective problem. Deep space functions as a containment vessel: cosmic-scale stimuli match the cosmic-scale dysregulation, and the absence of human peers eliminates the specific class of stressor (intimate witnessing) that has become intolerable. With the Starjammers she achieves a kind of operational equilibrium — high stimulation, low intimacy, role-mediated companionship. This is, in Hermanian terms, a partial Stage-One stabilization achieved by externalization rather than internal work.

**Cognitive style.** Expanded in scope, narrowed in object. She thinks at stellar scales; she does not think about Earth, her family, or the Avengers if she can avoid it. The cognition is mission-saturated, which prevents intrusive recall but also prevents integration. The Brood captivity — kidnapping, experimentation, bodily violation — is a re-traumatization, but it occurs inside a system already configured for tolerating extremity, and so is metabolized operationally rather than psychically.

**Self-concept.** Reorganized at scale. *Binary* is a self that is too large to be diminished, which is the point. The white-hole tap is, read symbolically, the most literal possible compensation for a developmental history of being told she could not have what she wanted: infinite energy on demand. The compensation works for as long as the power lasts.

**Defensive structure.** *Geographic avoidance* (a mature defense in some readings, an avoidant one in others — context-dependent) plus *grandiose compensation* via the powers themselves. Note: the grandiosity is structurally supported by actual cosmic capacity, which is why it does not meet criteria for NPD; remove the powers and the grandiosity does not persist as a personality structure but collapses, which is the next phase.

---

### Phase V — Warbird and the Alcoholic Bottom (mid-to-late 1990s)

**Affect regulation.** The compensation strategy fails. Powers reduce; Earth-orbit life resumes; the previously-quarantined affect — Marcus, Rogue, the Brood, the father — has no remaining container. She turns to ethanol, which is, pharmacologically, the most efficient available agent for blunting the entire affective range she has spent her life refusing to feel. The alcoholism is *not* hedonic; it is regulatory. She drinks to maintain the over-controlled surface that has been her operating system since childhood, now that the trauma-load has finally outrun the sublimative defenses.

**Cognitive style.** Degraded under intoxication, but more importantly, *narrowed under shame*. The intervention by Stark activates the original injustice template — male authority telling her to stand down — and her cognitive response is to reject the frame entirely, including its accurate content. She would rather be court-martialed by peers than receive correction from a man, even one structurally identical to her in addiction history. This is one of the most diagnostically revealing single decisions in the file: it shows that the *who-tells-her* matters as much as the *what-is-told*, and the wire runs through her father.

**Self-concept.** Bottoms out. The "Warbird" callsign is itself a self-diminution — bird, not the Marvel of Mar-Vell's line. She is, in this phase, closest to the *not-enough* child of Phase I, with the addition of decades of evidence she now interprets as proof. The recovery, when it comes, is structural rather than insight-based: she stops drinking by *exercising the same over-control* that produced the bottom, now redirected at the substance. This is durable — no documented relapse across all subsequent crises — and it is also limiting, because the underlying affect-quarantine architecture remains intact.

**Defensive structure.** Acute regression to *acting-out* (drinking) and *passive aggression* (the impaired sortie that endangers civilians is, read uncharitably, a way to communicate distress through dereliction). Recovery returns her to sublimation and reaction-formation, now *fortified* — and this fortification is what makes the next two decades both more functional and more rigid.

---

### Phase VI — *House of M* and the Corrective-Fantasy Years (2005–2011)

**Affect regulation.** Stabilized but pressurized. Sobriety holds; the regulatory style is now consciously maintained rather than unconsciously enacted. The *House of M* counterfactual injects a new and complicated affect she has not previously had to regulate: *envy of her own potential*. The experience of having been, in a reshaped reality, the world's most beloved hero produces a longing that is not nostalgia (she never had it) and not ambition (she already had ambition); it is closer to *grief for an unlived life*, and she does not have a vocabulary for it.

**Cognitive style.** Goal-saturated, increasingly future-oriented. Her cognition organizes around becoming-the-Carol-of-the-counterfactual, which is generative — it produces a decade of striving — but also subtly distorting, because it treats the present self as a draft of a better self rather than a person in her own right. The seam between "Carol" and "Captain Marvel" widens cognitively here even as it narrows behaviorally.

**Self-concept.** Aspirationally bifurcated. She knows what she wants to be and treats the gap as engineering problem. The trauma-residue is increasingly *managed* rather than *processed* — she is, in Hermanian terms, well into Stage Two (reconstruction) but skipping the grief-work that should accompany it.

**Defensive structure.** *Sublimation* at peak efficiency. *Identification with an ego-ideal* (the *House of M* self, and, later, Mar-Vell himself) supplies motivational structure. Reaction-formation against any felt-sense of remaining smallness becomes constant background tone — the cheer-forward declarativeness that will be most visible in the next phase.

---

### Phase VII — Captain Marvel, Aviator Culture, Mentorship (2012–2015)

**Affect regulation.** Best-integrated period of the published life. The mantle, the flight-suit iconography, the Banshee bar, the mentorship of Kamala Khan — these are not aesthetic choices but *containing structures* in Bion's sense. Each provides a holding environment in which affect can be experienced at low pressure: ritualized peer drinking-without-drinking, role-mediated nurturance, uniform-bound identity. She is, for perhaps the first time, *regulating through relationship* rather than through suppression or sublimation alone.

**Cognitive style.** Expanded by mentorship in a way solitary command had not permitted. Teaching Kamala forces her to articulate principles she had previously only enacted, and the articulation is itself integrative. She begins to access a slow, narrative cognition (telling Kamala her mistakes) alongside the fast tactical mode. This is the closest the file shows her to genuine *reflective function* in the mentalization sense.

**Self-concept.** Provisionally fused. "Carol" and "Captain Marvel" are nearer to one person than they have ever been, scaffolded by chosen-family and by the inherited dignity of the Mar-Vell name. The brain-lesion arc — choosing the mission knowing the cost to autobiographical memory — is the single most revealing self-concept datum in this phase: she experiences her self-continuity as *expendable in service*, which is either heroic or pathological depending on whether you weight the duty or the willingness-to-erase-the-self. Clinically, it is both. The integration is real and the willingness to dissolve it is also real, and the latter foreshadows Phase VIII.

**Defensive structure.** Mature defenses dominant — sublimation, altruism (mentorship), anticipation (mission-planning), humor (the dry aviator register). The healthiest configuration in the file.

---

### Phase VIII — *Civil War II* and the Authoritarian Overreach (2016)

**Affect regulation.** Decompensation under compounded grief. Rhodes' death and Jennifer Walters' coma arrive in close succession, and the regulatory system — which has never been able to occupy the middle register of sadness and fear — converts the grief into conviction at velocity. The Ulysses precognition is not the cause of the overreach; it is the *permission structure* that lets her enact a coping strategy she has been building since the Marcus event: *I will see the threat first; I will not be the one who failed to act*. Affect that should have been mourned is metabolized as policy.

**Cognitive style.** Splitting under stress, in the Kleinian sense. Dissenters become obstacles; nuance becomes obstruction; her own doubt becomes a security risk. The premature-closure tendency native to her cognitive style (action-bias under ambiguity) is, in this phase, no longer adaptive — the situation requires the slow consensus-building she has never been good at, and the cost of her not being good at it is borne by others.

**Self-concept.** Re-bifurcated under pressure, but in a new configuration: the integrated Phase-VII self is overridden by an emergent *command-self* that experiences peer dissent as betrayal-by-witnesses (the Marcus template, re-activated). She cannot, in this phase, distinguish between *being challenged* and *being unseen*, because her trauma-architecture treats them as the same thing.

**Defensive structure.** Regression along a familiar path — reaction-formation hardens into moral certitude; intellectualization escalates into ideology; splitting emerges; identification with the aggressor (the controlling parental structure she has spent her life resisting) becomes briefly enacted rather than resisted. Critically: *no return to substance use*. The sobriety wall holds; the regulatory pressure displaces sideways into governance instead. This is diagnostically important — it shows her defensive system as one of *displacement* rather than *collapse*, which is both why she survives her own bottoms and why her bottoms tend to be borne by others.

---

### Phase IX — *Life of Captain Marvel* and Matrilineal Integration (2018–)

**Affect regulation.** Re-stabilizing through grief-work the prior phases skipped. The dying-father storyline forces her into proximity with the original injustice in a register she cannot convert to action — Joseph is dying; there is nothing to fight. She is required, possibly for the first time in published life, to *sit* with affect she cannot operationalize. The discovery of Joseph's abuse of Marie reframes the developmental injustice as not merely *about her* but about a household — which is, paradoxically, freeing: she stops being the sole subject of the original wound.

**Cognitive style.** Narrative cognition ascends. She is doing autobiographical reorganization in real time — the Kree heritage retcon is, psychologically, an *integrative reframe* in which her powered self is revealed as continuous with her maternal line rather than as an alien graft on a small girl. Cognition is, for the first time, doing memory-work rather than mission-work.

**Self-concept.** Mythically reintegrated. The "Carol vs. Captain Marvel" seam is sealed at a deeper layer than the Phase-VII provisional fusion — she is now a person whose power has a *mother*, which is structurally different from a person whose power is an accident. This does not eliminate the trauma architecture; the wires remain. But it changes what the wires are wired to.

**Defensive structure.** Mature-tier dominant again, with the addition of something new: *grief tolerance*. Not large, not reliable, but present. This is the most prognostically significant change in the entire longitudinal record.

---

### Cross-Phase Synthesis

**Affect regulation, longitudinal arc.** From childhood over-control → dissociative quarantine → rageful breakthrough → geographic externalization → alcoholic suppression → sober rigidity → relational containment → command-displacement under grief → tentative grief-tolerance. The throughline is a system that has *never* been able to comfortably occupy the middle affective register and has cycled through increasingly sophisticated solutions to that incapacity. The current phase is the first in which she is building the capacity itself rather than substituting for it.

**Cognitive style, longitudinal arc.** Action-biased pattern-recognition has been the constant; what has varied is its coupling. Coupled to mission, it is exemplary command cognition. Coupled to unprocessed grief, it produces preemption. Coupled to mentorship, it produces articulation and reflection. The cognitive style itself is not the problem; the affective state it is yoked to determines whether it functions as gift or weapon.

**Self-concept, longitudinal arc.** Built by refusal, bifurcated by trauma, expanded by power, diminished by loss, aspirationally re-projected, provisionally fused, command-overridden, and finally mythically reintegrated. The arc is not linear but it is *cumulatively integrative* — each phase carries forward the residues of the prior ones, and the current self contains genuine sediment from all of them. The Phase-I refusal-child, the Phase-II bifurcated Ms. Marvel, the Phase-III rage-survivor, the Phase-IV cosmic exile, the Phase-V drinking Warbird, the Phase-VI aspirational striver, the Phase-VII mentoring aviator, the Phase-VIII command-isolate, and the Phase-IX integrated daughter are all still in there. Under stress, the older strata surface in roughly reverse-chronological order — which is why peers who have known her longest can predict her decompensations better than peers who have known only the recent integrated version.

**Prognostic implication.** The subject's psychological trajectory is one of progressively higher-order integrations interrupted by trauma-coherent regressions. The regressions are not failures of integration; they are *the form integration takes* in a system organized around refusal. She will, predictably, continue to cycle — and the cycle's amplitude is narrowing. The clinical task, were she ever to undertake it formally, would not be to eliminate the architecture but to add the missing middle register: to teach a woman who built herself out of *no* how to also say, occasionally, *I don't know*, *I'm afraid*, and *help me*. The Phase-IX evidence suggests she has begun this work without naming it as such, which is, characteristically, exactly how she would.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — SUBJECT: DANVERS, C.S.J.

*File §4. Clinical-formulation register. All diagnostic language is offered in DSM-5-TR / ICD-11 analog terms; the subject's hybrid biology and exposure to phenomena without terrestrial analog (memory-theft via mutant absorption, temporally-accelerated forced gestation, white-hole energy bonding) require some constructs to be extended beyond their nominal validation populations. Where this is done, it is flagged. This section is longitudinal: each condition is traced from prodrome through course, remission status, and current risk vector.*

---

## 4.1 PRIMARY DIAGNOSES (CURRENT)

### 4.1.1 Alcohol Use Disorder, Severe, In Sustained Full Remission

**ICD-11 6C40.2 / DSM-5-TR 303.90 analog. Remission >20 publication-years; no documented relapse across approximately six major continuity events including the death of a primary attachment figure (Rhodes, *Civil War II*) and elective neurosurgical-grade memory loss (*Captain Marvel* vol. 7 #14–17).**

*Etiology.* Onset is precisely datable to the Warbird era (*Avengers* vol. 3 #1–#7, with accelerant in *Iron Man* vol. 3 #7). The triggering matrix is textbook: (a) catastrophic narcissistic injury via power-loss following Binary descent; (b) re-entry into the precise peer group (Avengers) that had previously failed to witness her violation (the Marcus event); (c) absence of permitted grief channel — she had no language, in 1998-era heroic culture, for *I am less than I was and I am back among the people who watched me be taken*; (d) baseline trait obsessionality that had previously sublimated affect through mission-immersion was now operating against a diminished mission-capacity. Drinking filled the resulting affective vacuum.

*Symptom presentation in behavior.* Operational impairment is documented — combat flight while intoxicated, civilian endangerment during *Live Kree or Dead*. Tolerance escalation is implicit in the speed at which she progressed from social use to functional impairment. Denial structure was rigid and ego-syntonic; the intervention by Stark was rejected with maximal hostility *because* it came from a recovered alcoholic peer — i.e., from the one person whose mirror she could not refuse without violence. The court-martial that followed met the social-occupational impairment criterion in the most literal possible way: she was professionally adjudicated unfit by her own organization.

*Course and remission.* Recovery has been depicted as durable, austere, and absolute. There is no on-panel depiction of controlled drinking, "California sober," or social wine. The remission appears to be maintained via the same trait-rigidity that contributed to the original decompensation — a clinically common and clinically legitimate trade-off, but one that has *generalized*: the discipline that holds the bottle down also holds down a wider band of behaviors she has classified, perhaps over-broadly, as failure-coded. (See §4.4 on the personality scaffolding question.)

*Current risk.* Low for relapse under current conditions. Elevated under a specific scenario: simultaneous power-diminishment + loss of mentee + isolation from sober peers. The Warbird template is intact in memory; she watches for it; vigilance is protective but not sufficient under cumulative stressor load.

### 4.1.2 Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder, Chronic, Partially Compensated, with Dissociative Features (Historical)

**ICD-11 6B40 / DSM-5-TR 309.81 analog. Index traumas multiple, including at least one Criterion A event meeting the threshold of sexual violence (the Marcus event, *Avengers* #200, as reframed by Claremont in *Avengers Annual* #10). Chronic; partially compensated by sublimation, mentorship, and sobriety.**

*Index trauma inventory.* (1) *Forced impregnation, accelerated gestation, and forced parturition by a temporal entity who was her own offspring and her own captor* — the Marcus event. The compound violation here is unique in published heroic-cohort medical literature: bodily autonomy violation, reproductive coercion, gaslit witness-failure by chosen family, and a temporal-causal loop that frustrates ordinary trauma narrative. (2) *Prolonged captivity and forced biological experimentation by the Brood*, with implantation imagery that recapitulates the Marcus violation at species scale. (3) *Identity-and-memory absorption by Rogue* — a trauma without clean DSM analog; closest construct is severe depersonalization triggered by literal identity-theft, with the aggravating feature that the stolen self continued to walk around in another person's body, observable, for years. (4) *The Psyche-Magnitron explosion itself*, the originating biological violation that fused her genome with a foreign template without consent — retconned as congenital but experienced, at the time, as invasive. (5) *Brain lesion and elective memory loss* — self-inflicted in service to mission, but functionally a trauma to autobiographical continuity.

*Symptom presentation in behavior.* She does not present with classical re-experiencing on panel. This absence is itself diagnostically informative — it is consistent with the high-functioning combat-veteran presentation in which the disorder expresses through *behavior and worldview* rather than overt flashback or nightmare. Specifically:

- **Hypervigilance** is displaced from the somatic register (where it would manifest as startle, scanning, sleep disturbance — none of which she is shown indulging) to the *operational-political* register. She scans for threats-to-autonomy at civilizational scale; preemption (CWII) is hypervigilance writ as policy.
- **Avoidance** manifests not as phobic withdrawal but as *mission-immersion* — the unbroken operational tempo that prevents any unstructured interval in which intrusive material might surface. The DeConnick-era decision to fly the lesion-inducing mission rather than sit with the diagnosis is paradigmatic: when offered the choice between sustained reflection and accelerated duty with neurological cost, she chose the duty.
- **Negative alterations in cognition and mood** present as the constricted middle-affective register identified in §3 — sadness, ambivalence, and ordinary fear are the bands she cannot reliably occupy. This is not anhedonia; capacity for joy in flight, in mentorship, and in cosmic-scale wonder is preserved. It is selective affective constriction in the vulnerable bands only.
- **Alterations in arousal and reactivity** manifest as the incandescent-rage setting, almost always morally framed, and as the splitting-into-obstruction-frame under high stress.
- **Intrusive recapitulation** appears not as memory but as *action*. The CWII preemption regime is, formulated psychiatrically, the trauma reenacted from the agentic position: *I will be the one who sees the violation first, who acts, who is not overridden, who does not have to be congratulated by my chosen family while I am being taken.* The intrusive material has been metabolized into doctrine.

*Dissociative features, historical.* The original Ms. Marvel emergence (Conway, *Ms. Marvel* #1–#20) meets historical criteria for a dissociative identity presentation: discrete identity states, amnestic barriers between states, etiologically consistent with catastrophic somatic event layered on developmental invalidation. Largely integrated by Claremont's run and explicitly thematized as integrated by the Stohl run. Residue: she continues to refer to "Carol" and "Captain Marvel" as bifurcated objects under stress. This is now self-aware metaphor more than dissociative phenomenon, but the seam is observable.

*Course over time.* Chronic, with significant compensatory gains since circa the DeConnick run. Mentorship of Khan operates therapeutically (corrective parenting of the wounded child-self). Sobriety stabilizes the substrate. The Stohl-era matrilineal reconciliation closed a major open loop. The CWII episode, however, demonstrates that compensation is conditional: a sufficient combination of grief, threat, and authority can still produce trauma-driven decompensation in the *political-doctrinal* form rather than the affective-collapse form.

*Specifier note.* Meets criteria for **with dissociative symptoms (historical)** rather than current; current dissociative phenomena are minimal and largely metaphorical. Does NOT meet criteria for **with delayed expression** — onset of symptom evidence is roughly contemporaneous with index events.

### 4.1.3 Obsessive-Compulsive Personality Features, Sub-Threshold

**ICD-11 6D11.5 / DSM-5-TR 301.4 analog, sub-threshold. Does not meet full personality disorder criteria; scaffolding rather than impairment.**

Documented traits: preoccupation with order, perfectionism that interferes with task completion *only at the relational level* (not the operational level — operationally the perfectionism is functional), excessive devotion to work to the exclusion of leisure and intimacy, over-conscientiousness about moral matters, difficulty delegating, restricted affective expression, and a rigidity that has been both her defining strength and the rail along which her decompensations have traveled.

This is filed as trait-level rather than disorder because: (a) flexibility is demonstrable in mentorship contexts; (b) the perfectionism does not paralyze task completion; (c) interpersonal warmth, where present, is genuine rather than rule-bound; (d) miserliness — a diagnostic feature for the full disorder — is absent.

Clinical importance: this is the *substrate* on which the sobriety rests, on which the operational excellence rests, and on which the overreach also rests. It is non-negotiable and likely non-modifiable; treatment frame, if she ever entered one, would have to work *with* the trait rather than against it.

---

## 4.2 SUBSYNDROMAL AND TRAIT-LEVEL FINDINGS

### 4.2.1 Survivor Guilt (discrete subsyndromal feature)

Pronounced and historically traceable around three figures: Mar-Vell (whose name she took, whose death she did not prevent, whose mantle she carries with explicit awareness of inheritance-debt); Rhodes (the CWII catalyst, where guilt converted into doctrine in the space of hours); and Marie Danvers (the mother whose true nature was hidden, whose suffering at Joseph's hands Carol did not see in time). Not disorder-level; clinically significant because it is the *bridge* mechanism by which trauma load converts into action-doctrine. Survivor guilt is the affective currency she pays when she over-protects.

### 4.2.2 Moral Injury

Distinct from PTSD in the contemporary military-psychiatry literature; relevant here. The Marcus event is moral injury as much as trauma — it was the failure of *others* (the Avengers) to recognize an event as injury that produced the durable wound. The CWII arc is moral injury in the other direction: she became the perpetrator-of-overreach against her own chosen family, and the integration of that self-knowledge is incomplete. She has accepted the proposition *I was wrong* but the affective work of forgiveness-of-self appears unfinished.

### 4.2.3 Imposter Phenomenon

Sub-clinical but operationally relevant. Despite achievement record (USAF, NASA security chief, Avenger, cosmic-class operator), she is documented across multiple runs minimizing the pre-powered phase of her life. The *House of M* episode is diagnostic: presented with a counterfactual reality in which she was Earth's most beloved hero, her response was not *this is a fantasy* but *this is the life I should have had*. The implication — that the actual life, with all its achievement, was insufficient — is the imposter signature.

---

## 4.3 COMORBIDITY ANALYSIS

The three primary findings (AUD-in-remission, PTSD-chronic, OCPD-features) are not independent. They form a coherent etiological cluster:

1. The OCPD-features pre-date the heroic biography. They are likely temperamental and may have been reinforced by paternal authoritarianism (Joseph Danvers' household). They provided the cognitive style — control, order, work-primacy — that made USAF and NASA careers possible.
2. The PTSD layer was deposited by the cascade of bodily-autonomy violations beginning with the Psyche-Magnitron and culminating in the Marcus event.
3. The AUD episode was the failure mode that resulted when the OCPD scaffolding was overwhelmed by simultaneous power-loss (removing the sublimation channel) and re-immersion in the trauma-associated peer group (the Avengers).
4. Sobriety was achieved by *reinforcing* the OCPD scaffolding to load-bear what the sublimation channel had previously carried. This is why the personality structure now appears more rigid than her earlier-published self: it is doing more work.

This formulation predicts the CWII presentation: under sufficient stress (Rhodes' death + precognitive certainty + command burden), the over-loaded OCPD scaffolding does not collapse into substance use (the old failure mode, now blocked) but instead expresses as doctrinal rigidity and preemptive control. The same wall, redirected.

---

## 4.4 COURSE OVER TIME — LONGITUDINAL FORMULATION

**Phase I (pre-1968, pre-publication).** OCPD trait substrate established in invalidating paternal environment. Adaptive use: academic and physical achievement, military career path, escape velocity from family of origin.

**Phase II (1968–1980).** Powers acquisition trauma; dissociative identity-split as primary defense; integration of the split through the original Ms. Marvel run. The Marcus event at phase-end represents the catastrophic re-traumatization that overwhelmed all existing defenses simultaneously.

**Phase III (1981–1997).** Self-exile (Starjammers, Binary). Functionally equivalent to dissociative flight at interstellar scale. The cosmic power level masked the avoidance structure as adventure.

**Phase IV (1998–early 2000s).** Warbird descent. Substance-use decompensation under power-loss and re-immersion stress. Court-martial. Bottom. Sobriety. The reconstruction of self around reinforced trait-rigidity.

**Phase V (2005–2012).** *House of M* counterfactual installed as driving fantasy. Striving phase. Sobriety stable; doctrine stable; relationships gradually rebuilt; pro-registration alignment in Civil War prefigures the later overreach but is contained by collective context.

**Phase VI (2012–2016).** Captain Marvel mantle taken. Mentorship channel opens (Khan). Found-family with aviator subculture provides containment. Brain lesion and elective memory loss demonstrate the trait-rigidity working at its highest mode — duty over self-continuity, accepted clear-eyed.

**Phase VII (2016).** CWII decompensation in the political-doctrinal register. Sobriety holds. Relationships fracture. The failure mode has migrated, as predicted by the formulation, from substance to doctrine.

**Phase VIII (2018–).** Stohl-era matrilineal reconciliation closes the developmental loop. Integration of the human/Kree split at the mythic level. Post-CWII repair work ongoing and incomplete.

---

## 4.5 DIFFERENTIAL — WHAT SHE IS NOT, AND WHY

A rigorous differential is required because several diagnoses might be casually applied by an observer working from the surface presentation (cosmic power, command rigidity, the CWII episode). Each is here ruled out with the specific evidentiary basis.

### 4.5.1 NOT Narcissistic Personality Disorder

The surface case for NPD would cite: grandiosity, occupation of a literal "Captain Marvel" identity she elected to step into, the *House of M* counterfactual that explicitly figures her as Earth's most beloved, intolerance of dissent during CWII, and a habitual posture of certainty.

The diagnosis fails on every structural criterion. Her grandiosity is *achievement-justified*, not fantasized — she has, in fact, done the things; the self-presentation matches the operational record. Her empathy for the vulnerable is sustained, costly, and not contingent on audience — she mentors Khan in private and at expense to her own time, not for narcissistic supply. She tolerates being wrong, *eventually* and *painfully*, which is categorically not an NPD-compatible trait; the disorder is defined in part by the inability to integrate evidence of error without ego-collapse. Her shame-response is normative, not catastrophic. She does not exploit; she over-protects, which is structurally the opposite failure mode. The arrogance is *defensive* (a trauma-derived control posture) rather than *structural* (a fragile-grandiose self-organization).

### 4.5.2 NOT Antisocial Personality Disorder

The surface case would cite the CWII detentions — incarceration of persons for crimes not yet committed, willingness to override rights in service to her own threat-assessment. This is precisely the wrong frame. The CWII detentions are *ideologically driven and cause her remorse*. ASPD requires a pervasive disregard for the rights of others *without affective consequence to the actor*. Carol's actions in CWII produce documented anguish, fractured relationships she values, and post-hoc accountability work. ASPD does not feel that way from inside. She is, if anything, the *anti-type*: a person whose over-protective doctrine produces antisocial *outcomes* while her interior structure remains compulsively pro-social.

### 4.5.3 NOT Bipolar Disorder (any specifier)

The surface case would cite the Binary era — expansive mood, grandiose self-presentation, decreased need for sleep (she was operating in deep space without normal circadian inputs), pursuit of high-risk activity (Starjammers). The diagnosis fails because the expansiveness was *literal cosmic power*, not phenomenological mood elevation; the activity level was operational, not driven; and the episodes are not cyclical. There is no documented depressive pole that meets duration criteria, no inter-episodic euthymic baseline that would frame the Binary phase as episodic, and no family history (to the extent the Danvers family record is now legible) of mood-cycling disorder. Affect shifts across her published life are *reactive and trauma-coherent*, not episodic-autonomous. Bipolar is ruled out on construct grounds, not just symptom-count.

### 4.5.4 NOT Major Depressive Disorder

The surface case would cite the Warbird bottom. But the presentation at bottom was *irritable-avoidant-substance-using*, not anhedonic-vegetative. She did not lose capacity for action; she lost calibration of it. She did not lose interest in her core domains; she lost the right to practice them. She did not experience psychomotor slowing; she experienced behavioral disinhibition. The Warbird episode is an alcohol-use disorder with traumatic substrate, not a depressive episode. There is no documented period in her published life that meets the two-week duration criterion for major depression with the required symptom cluster.

### 4.5.5 NOT Borderline Personality Disorder

The surface case would cite the pattern of intense loyalty followed by abrupt withdrawal under perceived betrayal (Stark post-intervention, Avengers post-Marcus, Stark again post-CWII). This pattern is real but does not meet BPD criteria. The withdrawals are *consequent to specific, identifiable betrayal events* with proportionate (or over-proportionate but coherent) grounds; they are not idealization-devaluation oscillations driven by interpersonal anxiety. Identity disturbance, in the BPD sense of chronically unstable self-image, is absent — her self-concept is bifurcated (Carol/Captain Marvel) but each pole is stable; the issue is integration, not coherence. Affective instability is absent in the BPD sense (reactive shifts over hours within a day); her affective register is constricted, not labile. No self-injurious behavior. No chronic emptiness. The withdrawal pattern is better accounted for under disorganized-dismissive attachment with trauma-derived hypersensitivity to specific betrayal cues.

### 4.5.6 NOT Paranoid Personality Disorder

The CWII preemption regime might invite this differential. It fails because her threat-detection is *event-derived* (precognitive intelligence from Ulysses, in-universe legitimate) rather than baseline-suspicious. She extends trust by default; she over-extended it to her chosen family for decades. PPD requires pervasive distrust independent of evidence. Carol's pattern is the opposite: trust extended to default, weaponized doctrine activated only on identified threat-vector, withdrawal of trust only after specific betrayal.

### 4.5.7 NOT Current Substance Use Disorder

Active screening across post-recovery continuity finds no relapse evidence despite multiple stressors of sufficient magnitude to predict one in a less-disciplined recovery. Caffeine use is heavy and within cultural-occupational norms for military aviators. No documented misuse of analgesics post-injury. No process-addiction features (gambling, etc.) that would suggest substitution.

### 4.5.8 NOT a Dissociative Disorder, Current

The historical dissociative presentation (original Ms. Marvel split) has been integrated by narrative and clinical work across decades. Current self-bifurcation language is metaphorical, ego-syntonic, and consciously deployed. Amnestic phenomena post-lesion are organic-neurological, not dissociative. Depersonalization phenomena post-Rogue-absorption have not been re-presented in current continuity at clinically significant frequency or intensity.

### 4.5.9 NOT Autism Spectrum (a differential occasionally raised in casual analysis of high-rigidity, mission-focused command personalities)

Social communication is intact; reciprocal attunement to mentees (Khan) and to peer-emotion (her ability to read Stark's intervention as threatening *because* she correctly read his concern) demonstrates intact social-cognitive function. Restricted interests are occupational, not ASD-pattern. Sensory profile is unremarkable. Rigidity is trauma-derived and trait-OCPD, not ASD-derived.

### 4.5.10 Boundary case — Complex PTSD (ICD-11 6B41)

This is the differential that most nearly *applies* alongside, rather than instead of, standard PTSD. ICD-11 C-PTSD requires the PTSD core plus persistent disturbances in (a) affect regulation, (b) self-concept, and (c) relationships. Carol presents evidence for all three: constricted middle-affective register; bifurcated self-concept; the loyalty-withdrawal interpersonal pattern. The argument for adding the C-PTSD specifier rests on the *developmental* and *repeated* nature of her trauma exposure (paternal invalidation in childhood, then the cascade of adult violations). The argument against is that her self-concept disturbance and relational pattern, while real, do not reach the pervasive level the diagnosis requires; they are present under stress and recede under containment. **Best formulation: PTSD chronic with complex features, sub-threshold for full C-PTSD designation.** Clinically, the distinction matters because C-PTSD


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — DANVERS, C.S.J.

A field-observer's catalog. Organized by condition-state, then by register (somatic, vocal, kinetic, decisional, interpersonal). Cross-references to canon are abbreviated. The point of the Atlas is granularity: the things a tail with binoculars would log over a six-month observation window, the things a sparring partner learns in the second round, the things a friend learns over years.

---

## 1. BASELINE — CALM, UNOBSERVED, OFF-DUTY

The hardest state to catch her in. Subject does not have long contiguous stretches of true off-duty time; "calm" for her is the interstitial twenty minutes between operations, or the early morning before anyone else is awake.

**Somatic baseline.** Resting posture is *parade rest modified for civilian rooms* — weight even on both feet, hands clasped behind or loose at sides, shoulders down and back rather than rolled forward. When seated, she takes the chair facing the door; if there are two doors, she takes the corner. She does not slump. She does not cross her legs at the knee in the presence of strangers; ankles or uncrossed. Reading or watching something alone, she will pull a knee up to her chest — the only consistent "small" posture in her repertoire, observed only when she believes herself unwatched.

**Hands.** Right thumb worries the inside of the left wrist where the flight-jacket cuff sits — an old self-soothe so embedded she no longer notices it. When holding a coffee cup she wraps both hands around it even when it is not hot. She picks at the calluses on her palms during decision-pauses; the calluses regenerate because she trains daily.

**Vocal baseline.** Mid-alto, slightly gravelly in the morning, clears within an hour of waking. Cadence is clipped-but-warm with intimates, clipped-and-flat with strangers. She uses contractions liberally in private speech and almost never in official communications. Habitual verbal tics: "*Copy*" as acknowledgment (military residue, used even in grocery stores), "*roger that*" sarcastically when she disagrees, "*alright*" as a transition marker, the rising "*so*—" that signals she is about to take charge of a conversation that was meandering.

**Kinetic baseline.** Walks heel-strike, brisk, slightly longer stride than her hip mechanics warrant — she learned to keep up with taller male officers and never recalibrated. On stairs she takes them two at a time going up, one at a time going down (the descent is the dangerous direction; pilot training). She does not fidget with objects but she will reorient them: pens parallel to table edges, mugs handle-rightward, papers squared.

**Sleep architecture.** Short sleeper by training and by temperament — five hours is functional, four is tolerated, six is luxury. Wakes fully and instantly; no transition state. Sleeps on her back, arms at sides, in a t-shirt and shorts regardless of climate. Will not sleep in a room she has not walked the perimeter of. Reports (per Jessica Drew, off-record) that she keeps a glass of water on the bedside table she never drinks — it is a tripwire; if it is moved she will know.

**Eating.** Calorically high (metabolism elevated by the Kree substrate), preference for protein-dense and uncomplicated. Eats fast, finishes first, does not comment on food unless it is extraordinary. Will eat anything once. Coffee black, large, frequent; she stopped drinking after Warbird and has never developed a replacement vice in beverage form, which is itself a tell — most recovered drinkers substitute, she substituted into work.

**Reading material.** Aviation history, biographies of women pilots, occasionally hard SF. Keeps a paperback in her go-bag at all times. Dog-ears rather than bookmarks, which embarrasses her when caught.

---

## 2. MILD STRESS — IRRITATION, INCONVENIENCE, MINOR FRICTION

The bandwidth where most observation occurs, and where her tells are most reliable.

**The jaw.** First and most consistent tell across all eras and writers: the masseter clenches and the chin tucks half a centimeter. From the side, the mandible line sharpens; from the front, the lips compress without pursing. She does not know she does this. Anyone who has been on a team with her for more than three months reads it instantly.

**The exhale.** A single short nasal exhale through the nose — not a sigh, more a pressure-release. Often followed by the word "*alright*" at half-volume, addressed to no one. This is the verbal equivalent of resetting the avionics.

**The reframe.** Within thirty seconds of encountering a frustrating *interpersonal* problem, she will rephrase it as a *tactical* problem out loud. "Okay, what are we trying to actually accomplish here" is the canonical phrasing. This is intellectualization in real time and it works — for her. It frequently flattens the affective texture other people needed her to honor.

**Decisional habit.** Mild stress shortens her patience for consensus by roughly half. She will give a meeting one round of input and then summarize-and-decide. The summary will be accurate. The decision will be defensible. The people who were going to speak second will be annoyed.

**Physical displacement.** Will stand if she has been sitting. Will pace a short rectangular path — never circular, always cornered, pilot's habit of preferring known geometry. Will refill a coffee she has not finished.

---

## 3. MODERATE STRESS — OPERATIONAL PRESSURE, TIME-CRITICAL DECISIONS

**Voice.** Drops a quarter-tone, loses contractions, gains imperatives. She begins sentences with verbs: "Move." "Hold." "Tell me again." The warmth in private register is rationed out; she becomes courteous-cold with subordinates and curt with peers. She will still say *please* to civilians and to anyone under twenty.

**Body.** The hands stop fidgeting entirely. Stillness *increases* under operational stress — she becomes the calm point in the room because she has rerouted everything into cognition. Eyes track in deliberate sweeps rather than darting. She breathes deeper and slower (combat-aviator training, four-count box-breath, usually unconsciously). Skin flushes faintly across the upper cheekbones — the Kree substrate venting trace energy. Hair-trigger observers (Natasha, allegedly) read this as her power coming online before she calls it.

**Decisional habit.** Pattern-matches aggressively to prior engagements. Will name the analog out loud — "*This is the Brood pattern*", "*This is a Kree feint, not a real push*" — partly to brief, partly to confirm her own framing. Vulnerable to false-positive pattern lock-in when the new situation rhymes with an old trauma rather than an old tactic; the Marcus-coded scenarios are the canonical failure mode.

**Interpersonal.** Delegates decisively and specifically — names the person, names the task, names the time horizon. Does not micromanage *during* an op (she trusts trained operators) but will debrief them down to the rivets after.

**Tell of accumulating load.** When she has been running too hot for too many days, she begins ending sentences with the other person's name. "*Get it done, Rambeau.*" "*I hear you, Drew.*" The name-tag is a tell of her trying to keep the human-relationship channel open under a cognitive load that is closing it.

---

## 4. THREAT — IMMEDIATE COMBAT, ACUTE DANGER

**Pre-engagement.** Two-second stillness. She does not draw breath sharply; she lengthens her exhale and lowers her center of mass by an inch. The hands open from fists to flats — flat palms are her ignition posture, because the photonic discharge channels through them. There is a small tell at the corners of the mouth: not a smile, a *settling* of the lips, as if she has just put something down.

**During.** Flies offensive, not defensive. Closes distance rather than holding it. Prefers to put her own body between threat and bystanders even when this is tactically suboptimal — a behavior her trainers have called out and she has not corrected. Vocalizations during combat are short, almost monosyllabic: callsigns, directions, the occasional sharp "*MOVE*". She does not banter mid-combat. The wit is for before and after.

**Pain response.** Will not vocalize injury. Will alter movement to compensate without announcing it. Has been observed (Tony Stark, post-action telemetry, *Civil War II* era) to fly with broken ribs for forty minutes without comment. This is not stoicism for show — it is a deeply embedded prohibition against displaying somatic distress, traceable to a household in which her father read girls' pain as weakness.

**Power discipline.** Maximum-output discharges are visibly *expensive* to her now — she squints, the jaw locks, there is a half-second compression of her whole frame before the release. Post-DeConnick-lesion, she calibrates more conservatively in atmosphere; she will accept a longer fight over a higher discharge ceiling. The discipline is real but the temptation to over-power remains and shows up as a microscopic delay before throttling herself back.

**Threat to a third party she is responsible for.** This is where her tactical judgment most reliably breaks. She will take a hit she does not need to take, she will close a distance she should keep open, she will violate the briefed plan. Kamala-coded mentees produce the largest distortion. After the fact she will not concede the choice was suboptimal; she will say it was *correct*, and she will mean it.

---

## 5. INTIMACY — CHOSEN FAMILY, PRIVATE RELATIONSHIPS

**Access tiers.** She runs, functionally, three rings. *Outer* — colleagues, allies, the public. *Middle* — trusted operators, mentees, command-chain peers (Rhodey when alive; Steve; some of the Avengers). *Inner* — a count that has rarely exceeded four at a time (Jessica Drew is permanent; Monica Rambeau is permanent; Maria Rambeau was permanent; Kamala has been admitted; her sobriety sponsor, off-page, presumed permanent). Movement between tiers is slow inward and abrupt outward.

**Tells of inner-ring presence.** With inner-ring people she will: sit *adjacent* rather than across (the parade-rest dissolves; she puts her feet on furniture); use shortened nicknames she does not use elsewhere ("Jess", "Mon"); curse more colorfully; tell stories on herself; laugh from the belly rather than from the chest. The knee-to-chest posture from §1 appears in the presence of inner-ring people, which is the surest behavioral marker that she has admitted someone fully.

**Physical affection.** Sparing and emphatic. She does not casually touch — no incidental shoulder-brushes, no hand-on-arm during conversation. When she hugs, she hugs *hard*, both arms, full contact, slightly too long by polite-society standards; the contact is rare enough that she does not know how to make it brief. Will rest her forehead against another forehead in moments of high emotion (observed with Jessica Drew, with Kamala). Kisses the top of mentees' heads, an unconscious maternal gesture she would deny.

**Self-disclosure.** Rationed and oblique. She tells the *factual* outline of a story freely (the Brood, the Marcus event in clinical terms, the drinking) and the *affective* content almost never. She will say "*that was a bad time*" about Warbird and decline elaboration. Inner-ring people learn to read between the recited facts; she relies on them to do so and rewards the labor with deeper access.

**Romantic register.** Initiates rarely, accepts selectively, withdraws preemptively. The withdrawal usually takes the form of a mission that conveniently coincides with the relationship beginning to require maintenance. Partners who understand the calling (career military, fellow operators) last longer; partners who require her to be domestically present do not. With Rhodey: physical ease, sustained eye contact, the only relationship in which she was repeatedly observed *laughing first*. His death rewired her.

**Conflict in intimacy.** Asymmetrical. She runs hot during conflict and then *cold* — she will yell once, declaratively, then go silent and physically leave the space. The silence can last days. Repair, when it comes, is verbal and direct ("*I was wrong about X. I am sorry. I will do Y differently.*") but does not include affective elaboration. The other person is expected to accept the repair on its terms.

---

## 6. GRIEF

The most reliably hidden state, the most reliably destructive.

**Acute grief (first 48 hours).** Operational mode locks in. She does the logistics — calls, arrangements, public statements, the *work* of a death. Her competence in this period reads to outsiders as composure and to inner-ring observers as the warning. She does not eat regularly, drinks water only when handed it, sleeps not at all the first night and three hours the second. Will fly somewhere — anywhere — alone, in atmosphere, for the physical sensation of the airframe-equivalent stress on her body.

**The Rhodey signature.** Post-Rhodes-death (*Civil War II* opening), the documented behavioral progression was: 6 hours of operational competence, public statement delivered without affect break, private 20-minute disappearance (presumed somatic discharge — flight, weeping, neither confirmed), return with a *plan*. The plan was the overreach. Grief metabolized as conviction is her most dangerous pathway.

**Chronic grief.** She integrates losses into the work. Mar-Vell's name on her chest is the literal version. Maria Rambeau's absence reorganized her relationship to Monica. The losses accumulate as *standards she now holds herself to* rather than as wounds she lets close. This is the OCPD-spectrum trait scaffolding her psychology: grief becomes obligation becomes rigidity.

**Tells of unmetabolized grief.** Increased sentence-clipping. Disappearance of contractions even in private speech. The thumb-on-wrist self-soothe doubles in frequency. She will reread the same paragraph of a book multiple times without registering it. She will go to a hangar at 0300 and run pre-flight checks on aircraft she has no intention of flying.

**Crying.** Documented rarely on-panel and always in inner-ring privacy. She cries *silently*, hands at sides, face still, tears tracked. Does not sob, does not gasp. Will turn her face away even from people she trusts. The crying is brief — minutes, not hours — and is followed by a hard reset (face washed, hair re-tied, return to the world).

---

## 7. VICTORY

The state that exposes her humility-vs-grandiosity tension most clearly.

**Immediate post-action.** Underclaims. Will deflect to the team, to the pilot of the second airframe, to the analyst who flagged the pattern. The deflection is genuine — she remembers who did what and is scrupulous about credit — but it is also a defense against the vertigo of having been the decisive instrument. She is not comfortable being thanked face-to-face by civilians; she nods, says "*just doing the job, ma'am*", and exits.

**Celebration.** Will attend, briefly. Stands near a wall. Holds a glass of seltzer with lime — the *visual* of a drink, the absence of alcohol; this is a deliberate sobriety practice she has used for 25+ years. Leaves early with a credible excuse. The pilots' bar (the Banshee cohort) is the exception — there she will stay until close, tell flight stories, sing badly, and be the last to leave.

**Private victory.** Sleeps better that night. Cooks something elaborate the next morning (the only condition under which she cooks elaborately — victory-omelets are a documented Drew-household phenomenon). Calls her mother.

**Risk profile of victory.** Lowest of any state. She does not get sloppy after wins; if anything, she becomes more vigilant for the *next* threat. The post-victory cortisol-drop that catches most operators does not seem to catch her, which is itself a tell — she does not let herself fully land in the win.

---

## 8. DEFEAT

**Tactical defeat (mission failure, bystanders lost).** Public composure intact. Private aftermath: she will personally write to the families. Handwritten when possible. Names spelled correctly. Will fly out to attend funerals when invited and stand at the back. Will not attend uninvited.

**Personal defeat (being wrong, being called on it).** This is where the rigidity load-bears hardest. First reaction is *defense* — she will marshal the reasoning, the evidence, the constraints she was operating under. Second reaction, hours to days later, is *withdrawal* — she will get quiet, get scarce, run perimeter on her own thinking. Third reaction, days to weeks later, is *concession*, delivered cleanly and without theater: "*I was wrong. Here is what I now think. Here is what I will do differently.*" The concession is real. The cost of producing it is high enough that she does not produce it often.

**The Tony intervention template.** When confronted by someone she trusts with a truth she cannot yet metabolize, she will *escalate* — accuse the confronter of betrayal, leave the room, leave the team, leave the city if necessary. The escalation buys her the distance she needs to come back to the truth on her own timeline. People who have known her long enough know to absorb the first volley and wait. People who do not know this lose her.

**Loss of capability (depowering, injury, benching).** This is the Warbird substrate and the state she most fears. Tells: increased irritability, contempt-flickers in expression (rare baseline behavior, diagnostic when present), tactical second-guessing of operators in roles she would have held, withdrawal from inner-ring contact. She knows this about herself now. She has standing instructions to certain inner-ring people (Jessica, Monica) to *not* leave her alone in this state. Whether she follows the instructions to invite them in is variable.

---

## 9. RITUALS, ROUTES, REPETITIONS

**Morning.** Wake before dawn when possible. Push-ups and pull-ups to a fixed count (not maximum — she stops at the count even when she could do more; the discipline is in the stopping). Coffee. Twenty minutes of news consumption, prioritizing international and aerospace. Calls or texts to inner-ring at predictable intervals (Monday morning to Monica, Friday evening to Jessica, daily check to Kamala when Kamala was in operational rotation).

**Pre-flight ritual.** Walks the airframe even when she is the airframe. Touches the nose of any aircraft she boards, palm flat, two seconds — pilot superstition she has never broken. Verbalizes her flight plan to herself, even on routine sorties.

**Anniversary behaviors.** Quieter than usual in the week of Mar-Vell's death-anniversary. Drinks (water) a toast at the Banshee bar on the anniversary of the first sober year.
