**Time.** Twenty-four hours of held judgment, before any irrevocable action, will produce different decisions than the first ninety minutes. Any process that can build in a hold buys her the use of her own better mind. This is the single most replicable protective practice available.

---

## 5. CALMING PROFILES — HOW SHE IS BROUGHT DOWN

She does not calm via comfort. She calms via *task*, *witness*, and *legibility*.

**Task.** Give her something to do with her hands or her training. The aviator's checklist behavior is real; running a sequence — pre-flight, weapons check, mission brief — restores her access to her own competence and lowers the systemic arousal. Idleness during distress is contraindicated; she will spiral inside it.

**Witness.** A single trusted person, in the room, not speaking unless asked, doing something parallel — drinking coffee, working on their own laptop, reading. The proximity without demand is the medicine. She will eventually speak; the speaking is what processes the affect. The witness's job is to be there long enough for the speaking to happen, and to not flinch when it does.

**Legibility.** Tell her what is going on. *Three things happened in the last hour; here they are in order; here is what we know and what we don't.* Ambiguity sustains her arousal; structure dissolves it. A whiteboard, a tactical map, a written timeline — physical legibility, not verbal — is the most effective format.

**What does not work:** physical comfort without warning, soft voices, telling her to breathe, telling her she is safe (the word *safe* is a tripwire; she does not believe in it as a category and the word reads as condescension), removing her from operational context, sedation, anything resembling a debrief by a person she has not chosen.

---

## 6. DESTABILIZATION PROFILES — HOW AN ADVERSARY WOULD BREAK HER

Documented for protective vigilance. The sequence below is the path of greatest efficacy; allies should monitor for any subset appearing in operational context.

1. **Isolate her from her sober peers and her chosen family.** Manufactured missions that separate, schedules that prevent ritual contact, information warfare that introduces doubt between her and Jessica Drew specifically.
2. **Degrade her access to mentorship.** Threaten Kamala in a way that requires Carol to keep distance "for her safety." Remove the corrective loop.
3. **Diminish her capability without removing it entirely.** Partial power suppression is worse than full; it triggers the Warbird substrate without giving her the dignity of total grounding.
4. **Introduce predictive intelligence about catastrophic harm.** Real or fabricated. Watch the preemption logic engage.
5. **Stage a violation that her chosen family fails to recognize as a violation.** The Marcus shape. Even partial replication of this geometry will produce disproportionate response and durable damage to her support system.
6. **Offer her a drink at the bottom of the sequence.** Not because she will take it — she will not — but because the offer is the final insult and the refusal will cost her energy she no longer has.

The countermeasure is collective: a network around her that is briefed on the sequence, watching for the early steps, and authorized to intervene before the late ones. No single ally can hold the perimeter; she has too many doors.

---

## 7. RECONCILIATION AND REPAIR PROFILES

After a rupture — and there will be ruptures — she does not respond to apology. She responds to *changed behavior demonstrated over time without comment*. The person who has wronged her must do the work, visibly, for months, without asking for credit or relief, before the door reopens. When it reopens it opens fully; she does not do partial reconciliation. The all-or-nothing structure that supports her sobriety supports this too.

The Tony Stark relationship is the case study: rupture, years of distance, slow re-entry through demonstrated competence and demonstrated accountability on both sides, eventual operational trust never quite restored to pre-rupture intimacy. This is the realistic ceiling on repair, not the floor. Allies should not expect that what was broken returns identical; they should expect that what returns is functional, scarred, and survivable.

The single most effective repair gesture across her published life: *naming the specific thing that was missed.* Not *I'm sorry,* but *I'm sorry I didn't see what was happening to you when Marcus took you. I should have seen it. I failed you specifically there.* The specificity is the medicine. Generality reads as evasion.

---

## 8. PROGNOSTIC NOTE ON LEVERAGE

She is, by the measure of this file, harder to break than to bend and harder to bend than to redirect. The leverage profile favors the patient adversary and the patient ally equally; her structure does not yield to force, only to time and specificity. The genuine vulnerability is not in any single wire but in the *combination* of isolation, diminishment, and predictive pressure — the three-vector attack that produced *Civil War II* and would produce its sequel under similar conditions.

The protective inverse is therefore not the fortification of any one wire but the maintenance of her *network* — Jessica, Kamala, Monica, the Banshees, the living memory of Rhodey carried by those who knew them both. The network is the thing. She has built a self out of refusal; the network is the thing that lets her, occasionally, put the refusal down. Anyone who weakens the network weakens her. Anyone who strengthens it strengthens her more than any direct intervention could.

The file recommends, for protective purposes, the following standing practice: *no operationally significant decision by Subject within twenty-four hours of a precipitating event, where any member of the trusted network is reachable.* This single rule, applied consistently, would have prevented most of her published worst calls. It is the closest thing this dossier has to a load-bearing recommendation.

*— End section. Cross-reference §3 (Psychological) and §4 (Psychiatric) of the parent workup for the developmental and clinical grounding of the leverage profile above.*


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# 6. STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE — THE ASSET LEDGER

*A complete inventory of what this subject brings to bear: the somatic, cognitive, characterological, relational, material, and institutional resources that keep her vertical and make her, by any honest tally, one of the most consequential operators on the board. Read against §3–§4: these are not the absence of her pathologies; many of them are the same machinery turned to load-bearing use.*

---

## 6.1 SOMATIC & PHYSICAL ASSETS

**Power baseline (current Captain Marvel era).** Class 100 strength fluctuating upward under absorption load; sustained atmospheric flight at hypersonic speeds; full-spectrum durability extending to vacuum, re-entry, and direct energy-weapon fire; photonic blasts at sub-stellar yields; the energy-absorption channel that converts incoming damage into output — the single most strategically valuable defensive trait in the Avengers roster because it inverts the threat model: hitting her makes her stronger. Sub-light interplanetary travel without life support. Limited bio-electromagnetic "seventh sense" (intermittent across eras; functionally a low-bandwidth threat-anticipation channel — not precognition proper, but a calibrated unease that has saved her life enough times to be trusted).

**Binary substrate, latent.** The white-hole tap is not gone; it is dormant. Has surged back under specific cosmic conditions (*Avengers* vol. 4, briefly; *Avengers: The Enemy Within*). Operationally this means her ceiling is unknown to her and to opponents — a deterrent value distinct from raw output.

**Hybrid Kree physiology (per *Life of CM* retcon).** Accelerated healing; resistance to most terrestrial toxins, pathogens, and radiation; reduced sleep requirement (functional on four hours, optimal on six); preserved peak conditioning with minimal maintenance training. Practical effect: she is a 24-hour asset in crisis without the cognitive degradation that limits her peer pilots.

**Trained-pilot somatic suite (pre-power, never lost).** G-tolerance built over USAF career — she can pull and sustain accelerations that would gray-out unenhanced pilots even *without* her durability factor compensating; this matters because it means her flight reflexes were tuned in an unforgiving school before powers arrived to forgive errors. Manual instrument flying, multi-engine, rotary, experimental airframes. Aerial gunnery. Hand-to-hand at military-instructor level (Air Force CQC base, augmented by Avengers-era drilling with Captain America and the Black Widow cadre; she spars regularly, demonstrably, across decades — not a once-trained operator, a *currently* trained one).

**Pain tolerance.** Atypical even for the cohort. Endured Brood implantation, Psyche-Magnitron incineration, and atmospheric-flight cranial lesion without operational withdrawal. The trait cuts both ways (see §3 re: fear-as-noise), but as an asset in extremis it is near-unmatched.

---

## 6.2 COGNITIVE & TECHNICAL ASSETS

**Aviation and aerospace expertise.** Test-pilot–grade airframe knowledge; NASA-tier orbital mechanics; can read and improvise off mission profiles for craft she has never flown by analogy from first principles. Has crewed Shi'ar, Kree, and Skrull vessels in field conditions.

**Intelligence tradecraft.** USAF Intelligence career (pre-NASA) plus chief of security at Cape Canaveral — the latter a counterintelligence post against a Cold-War-era threat surface that included Soviet, AIM, and Hydra penetration attempts. She knows how covers are built, run, and broken; she vets people the way a case officer does, in layered passes, often without the subject noticing.

**Languages.** English (native, Boston-Irish substrate occasionally surfacing under stress or alcohol-era footage); functional Kree (acquired post-fusion, accent imperfect by Kree-Pama standards); conversational Shi'ar (Starjammers era); operational Russian (USAF Intel period); recognition-level Skrull, Spanish, French. Comprehension under universal-translator failure remains a known operational floor.

**Writing and journalism craft.** Edited *Woman Magazine* under J. Jonah Jameson; freelanced widely; later authored a memoir-adjacent volume. Communicates in clean declarative prose; can run press, brief leadership, draft after-action reports without staff. The asset is not "she can write" — it is that her self-articulation under public pressure is *trained*, which is why her press conferences land and her internal Avengers memos are quoted back at her.

**Tactical pattern-recognition.** Inductive, fast, action-biased (§3). Under time pressure she is among the best in the cohort; with hours to plan, she is good; with weeks and committee, she is impatient but functional. The strength is the *speed at which she sees the shape of a fight* — terrain, hostile force composition, civilian vectors, ally positioning — and converts it to assignments in a single sentence.

**Command competence.** Has held senior field command of the Avengers, the Ultimates, Alpha Flight Space Program, and various joint operations. Knows how to write a watch schedule, run a logistics tail, manage media-mil interface, and conduct an after-action without scapegoating. The CWII failure is not a command-competence failure; it is a moral-framework failure executed *through* high command competence, which is precisely why it did as much damage as it did.

---

## 6.3 CHARACTEROLOGICAL ASSETS

**Refusal as a generative trait.** The defining negative — *no, not you* — was metabolized into a positive structural disposition: she does not accept ceilings imposed by others. This is the engine under every meaningful achievement in the file. When deployed against external limits (Kree military hierarchy, Avengers gatekeeping, the Marcus apologia) it is unambiguously good. The work of her life is learning to direct it.

**Sustained sobriety as discipline-template.** Twenty-plus published years dry, through losses that would justify relapse (Rhodey; the lesion arc; CWII fallout). The discipline is real and transferable: she runs other domains of her life on the same architecture — accountability partners (Jessica Drew functions as such, formally or not), routine, refusal of solitary brooding-with-bottle, willingness to call a meeting and *say it out loud*. This is, statistically, the rarest and most durable resilience marker in the dossier.

**Capacity for post-hoc accountability.** Post-CWII she did not litigate her position to death; she absorbed the verdict, took the isolation, kept working, and recalibrated. Post-Marcus (Claremont era) she stood in a room of her chosen family and named what they had done. These are not the moves of someone who cannot tolerate being wrong; they are the moves of someone who tolerates it slowly, expensively, and *truly*.

**Mentorship as restorative practice.** With Kamala Khan she has invented a parental register her own father never modeled — patient, encouraging, willing to be looked up to without weaponizing the look. The relationship is genuinely two-way; Kamala has corrected her and been heard. Mentorship is not just an output of her character but an *input* to it: caring for a younger version of herself stabilizes the older one.

**Humor under fire.** Dry, fast, often self-directed. The aviator deadpan is a regulatory tool — it lets her hold a scene without escalating it, lets subordinates exhale, signals that the situation is bounded. Notable that she keeps it even when frightened; it is one of her tells *against* full splitting (when the humor goes, the perimeter is closing).

**Loyalty depth.** When she is in, she is in for decades — Jessica Drew, Monica Rambeau, Rhodey, the Banshees. The loyalty survives her own withdrawals; she returns to these people, repairs at cost, does not let bonds rot in silence even when she has been the one to break them. This is rarer than her public profile suggests.

**Moral seriousness.** She experiences ethics as load-bearing, not decorative. The same trait that produced the CWII overreach also produces her refusal to take shortcuts that lesser commanders take routinely (no torture-by-proxy; no civilian-cost optimization; no off-books deniable ops). Her errors are public because her ethics are public.

**Service-orientation toward the weaker party.** Consistent across every era and every writer. Not performed; structural. She moves toward the endangered civilian, the abused subordinate, the bullied teenager. This is the trait Claremont saw and built the post-Marcus arc around; it is the trait DeConnick centered; it survives even her authoritarian episodes intact, which is diagnostically important (cf. §4 differential against antisocial/narcissistic).

---

## 6.4 RELATIONAL & SOCIAL CAPITAL

**Chosen family — primary tier.**
- *Jessica Drew (Spider-Woman):* the longest-running peer intimacy in her file. Mutual disclosure rate higher than with any other relationship; functions as her honest mirror, her sobriety witness in practice if not in label, and the person most likely to be told the *actual* internal weather. Reciprocal — Carol is Jessica's same.
- *Monica Rambeau:* the only person who has held the Captain Marvel name from her and given it back; the relationship survived the handoff in both directions, which is a non-trivial test.
- *James Rhodes (deceased, CWII):* romantic and operational partner; the loss is unhealed but metabolized; the relationship modeled for her that a peer-equal soldier-partner was *possible*, which is a template she now holds.
- *Kamala Khan:* mentee/quasi-daughter; restorative bond (see 6.3).

**Chosen family — secondary tier.** Tony Stark (repaired across multiple breaks, currently functional); Steve Rogers (mutual professional regard, slower intimacy); the Banshee pilots (chosen-family bar-culture); Wendy Kawasaki (ground crew, longtime trusted civilian); Tracy Burke (her old journalist mentor, a mother-coded relationship that pre-dates the Marie reconciliation and may have prefigured it).

**Institutional access.**
- *Avengers* (founding-era seniority by tenure, multiple chairmanships).
- *S.W.O.R.D.* and *Alpha Flight Space Program* (commanded the latter; permanent network).
- *USAF and NASA legacy networks* — old colleagues now in senior positions; she can still place a call.
- *Kree contacts* (post-*Life of CM*) — fraught but real.
- *Starjammer rapport* (Binary era; cosmic-tier rolodex including Lilandra-era Shi'ar contacts, the Brood-survivor underground, and various spaceways operators).

**Public capital.** She is one of the most publicly legible Avengers — uniform, callsign, mission profile, recognizable iconography. This is operationally useful (de-escalation by recognition; civilian compliance in evacuations) and personally costly (no anonymity floor). She has learned to spend the capital deliberately: press appearances for causes (women in aerospace, veteran support), not for self.

**Reputation among adversaries.** Read by Kree, Skrull, and most terrestrial threats as a *credible deterrent*. The Binary ceiling functions as a strategic-ambiguity asset (see 6.1). Even Thanos-tier opponents treat her as a priority target, which — counterintuitively — is an asset, because it means she is read into threats early.

---

## 6.5 MATERIAL & LOGISTICAL ASSETS

**Quarters.** Maintains an apartment in New York (currently); has held quarters at Avengers Mansion, Avengers Tower, and aboard Alpha Flight Station. Practical minimum-footprint personal goods — go-bag culture from military life, never fully shed. Apartment kitchen functional but underused; coffee setup overbuilt (single-origin, hand-grinder, kettle with temperature control — one of her few connoisseur indulgences).

**Personal kit.** Flight jacket (the iconic leather, replaced periodically but always the same cut — sentimental object as much as garment); dog tags (her father's *and* her own, worn together — a reconciliation artifact post-*Life of CM*); the Hala Star sash; a small number of photographs kept physically rather than digitally (Maria, Mar-Vell, Rhodey, the Banshees, Kamala). A modest library skewing aviation history, naval/aerospace memoir, and — quietly — poetry (she does not advertise this).

**Financial.** Avengers stipend; USAF pension; royalties from *Woman Magazine* and her memoir; consulting income from aerospace work. Not wealthy, comfortably solvent, does not optimize. Spends on others — Kamala's college fund quietly seeded; Banshee bar tabs covered; veteran-support donations consistent.

**Technological access.** Stark-built comms (despite their history, Tony keeps her loop current); SWORD-issue field tools; Kree biotech for power-output management. Pilot's certifications kept current on civilian airframes she no longer needs to fly — a discipline-tell.

**The cat (Chewie / Goose).** Flerken; effectively a pocket-universe and a tactical asset in its own right; companion animal that doubles as deep-space contraband storage. Bond is genuine — she talks to it. Diagnostically: she keeps a non-human creature whose presence does not require her to perform competence.

---

## 6.6 RESILIENCE FACTORS — WHY THE STRUCTURE HOLDS

**Sublimation channel is wide and well-paved.** Most trauma survivors lack a socially sanctioned outlet large enough to absorb their affect; she has *cosmic-scale combat* and *command of others* as legitimate, valorized, continuous outlets. The fit between her pathology and her job is unusually high. This is protective.

**Sobriety scaffolding generalizes.** The cognitive-behavioral architecture she built to stay dry — naming the urge, calling a person, removing the means, refusing the story that justifies the drink — has migrated into her management of other compulsions (over-control, isolation, certainty). She does not always win, but she has the *tools*, and she knows the tools exist, which most people do not.

**Multiple integrated identity reconciliations.** She has done the work — *Life of CM*, post-CWII, post-Warbird — of integrating split selves. Each reconciliation strengthens the next: the matrilineal integration with Marie made the post-CWII isolation survivable because she had practiced taking hard truth and metabolizing it without dissolving.

**A diverse, deliberately maintained support net.** Jessica, Monica, Kamala, Rhodey-while-living, the Banshees, Tracy Burke, Wendy. She has more than one person, in more than one register (peer, mentor, mentee, professional, civilian), and she has practiced *calling* them, which sober people learn early and other people often never do.

**Embodied self-knowledge about her own escalation ladder.** She can name, now, the difference between operational cool and reaction-formed declarativeness; the difference between firm command and splitting-driven preemption. She does not always self-correct in time, but the watchtower is staffed. Post-CWII this has measurably improved.

**Capacity to sit with mortality.** The lesion-arc final mission — knowing she would lose recent memory, going anyway — is not bravado; it is a developed capacity to accept loss of self in service of mission *without* dissociating. Distinct from her earlier dissociative phenomena; this is integrated sacrifice, not split survival.

**Mentorship as ongoing repair.** Each interaction with Kamala — and to a lesser extent with younger Avengers, with the Banshees, with the SWORD juniors — re-grounds her in the version of herself she most wants to be. This is not performative; it is genuinely regulatory. She is calmer after she has been useful to a younger person.

**Humor preserved through every era.** That her dry register has survived the Marcus event, the Brood, the alcoholism, the lesion, and CWII is itself a resilience signal. When the humor goes, the perimeter is closing — but it has, so far, always come back.

**Real ethical core, not a performance of one.** This is the bedrock asset and the reason peers absorb her withdrawals and wait for her: she means it. The values are not for show. When she is wrong, she is wrong on *behalf* of something she actually believes serves the vulnerable, which is recoverable. Operators who are wrong on behalf of themselves are not.

---

## 6.7 THE LOAD-BEARING SYNTHESIS

The asset ledger is unusually *coherent*: somatic capability, cognitive training, characterological discipline, relational depth, institutional access, and material baseline all point the same direction and reinforce each other. She is not a brittle high-performer running on a single faculty; she is a structurally sound one running on a deep, redundant stack.

The same trait inventory that — under §3–§4 stress — produces overreach, isolation, and command-failure also produces, under nominal conditions, one of the most durable, ethically serious, and operationally formidable assets the cohort possesses. The instruments are dual-use. The maintenance question is not *whether she has the resources* — she emphatically does — but *who is standing close enough to call her name when the perimeter starts closing*.

On the present evidence, that person exists; usually more than one; and she has learned, expensively, to pick up the phone.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: DANVERS, CAROL SUSAN JANE
## §6. FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION

> *"She does not fall apart. She compresses, hardens, and accelerates. Then a load-bearing thing breaks somewhere out of frame, and only after that does she look — briefly — like a person in trouble. By then the damage is done and someone else is usually paying for it."*

This section maps how the subject breaks. The headline finding, derived across forty-plus years of canon, is that Danvers is not a *collapser*. Most decompensation in the Avengers cohort follows a recognizable arc of visible deterioration — affect destabilizes, performance drops, the subject becomes legibly unwell to those around them, and intervention becomes possible. Danvers inverts this. Her failure mode is **escalation under load**: as internal pressure rises, *external performance also rises*, becoming brittler, more declarative, more morally absolutist, and more operationally effective right up until the moment a discrete catastrophic act resolves the pressure for her. The collapse, when it comes, is usually *retroactive* — a thing she and others have to look back at and identify as having already happened.

This makes her exceptionally dangerous in command and exceptionally hard to intervene with. It is also the single most important pattern in this file for anyone tasked with working alongside her in crisis.

---

### 6.1 The Escalation Ladder — Granular Behavioral Signature

The five-stage ladder sketched in §5 requires expansion. Each rung has a *somatic*, *verbal*, *interpersonal*, and *operational* signature. A trained observer can map her position on the ladder within thirty seconds of a room entry.

**Rung 1 — Baseline (Compensated Operating Mode).**
*Somatic:* Loose-shouldered, hands at rest, weight evenly distributed; she leans into chairs rather than sitting upright in them. Standard pilot's resting heart rate, slow blink. Eats in company, sleeps roughly six hours, accepts coffee. Hair worn down or in a loose tie.
*Verbal:* Dry, clipped humor with aviator-bar cadence; willing to be teased; uses contractions; calls people by first names and nicknames (*Jess, Rhodey, Kamala, Tones*). Profanity-comfortable, off-duty register.
*Interpersonal:* Initiates contact. Touches forearms, claps shoulders, hugs Kamala without preamble. Allows herself to be the one being looked after in small ways (Jessica refilling her glass, Monica handing her a jacket).
*Operational:* Delegates without monitoring. Will leave a mission early if it is in capable hands. Sleeps on planes.

**Rung 2 — Mild Stress (Cool Override Activated).**
*Somatic:* Posture squares. Jaw set, with a specific micro-tell — she shifts her lower jaw slightly forward and to the right before speaking on a hard topic; this is consistent across decades of art direction by independent pencillers and is treated here as a reliable physiological signature, not an art-style artifact. Hair goes up. Flight jacket goes on indoors. Resting hand moves to hip or to the back of a chair — *contact with structure*.
*Verbal:* Sentences shorten. Contractions drop. First-names give way to call-signs and surnames. Humor narrows to single sardonic beats rather than back-and-forth.
*Interpersonal:* Still warm at the perimeter (Kamala, Banshees) but the warmth becomes one-directional — she gives, refuses receipt. Deflects "how are you" with mission-status.
*Operational:* Begins double-checking subordinates' work without telling them. Sleep contracts to four hours. Coffee in, alcohol-substitute rituals (black coffee, ice water, cigarettes if available) up.

**Rung 3 — Moderate Stress (Tactical Reframing).**
*Somatic:* Standing meetings preferred. She paces a defined rectangle — almost always pacing *toward and away from a window or exit*, a behavior that reads, in surveillance terms, as a flight-trained body managing the impulse to take off. Eats standing, eats less, but eats — sobriety discipline holds the meal in place even as appetite falls. Resting heart rate elevates roughly 10–15 bpm above her trained baseline; visible at the throat hollow under stage lighting.
*Verbal:* Personal questions get tactical answers. "Are you okay?" becomes "We're on schedule." Uses the passive voice about her own feelings (*the situation is frustrating*) and the active voice about others' (*Stark is being obstructive*). Begins to use the word **"need"** in places where "want" or "intend" would be honest — *I need you to stand down* — a linguistic tell that the conversation has been reframed from request to operational directive.
*Interpersonal:* Inner circle contracts to two or three people, usually subordinates who will not push back (the Banshee pilots, Kamala) rather than peers who will (Jessica, Rhodey when alive, Monica). Calls to Jessica drop off; texts go unreturned for days, then arrive in bursts at 0300.
*Operational:* Begins making unilateral calls inside collaborative structures. Will brief a team on a decision rather than convene one to make it. Sleep at three hours, in uniform, on a couch in the operations area rather than in quarters. The flight jacket is now never off.

**Rung 4 — High Stress (Moral Hardening).**
This is the rung at which she becomes *dangerous to the project she is trying to protect*. The Civil War II detention regime sits here for most of its duration.
*Somatic:* Powered-state idle becomes visible — a faint photonic shimmer at the hairline and knuckles even at rest, indicating the energy-absorption substrate is running hotter than baseline. She flies short distances she would normally walk. Will hover an inch off the floor in argument without noticing. Eyes go to the harder, brighter cast (canonically rendered as the "photonic" eye-state); pupils less responsive to light changes. Sleep at one to two hours, frequently airborne — she patrols in lieu of resting. Stops eating in company; eats alone or not at all. Sobriety discipline still holds and now becomes load-bearing — she will not drink, but she also will not stop *anything else*.
*Verbal:* Speech becomes declarative-imperative. The word **"have to"** replaces "should." Uses the future-certain tense about contested predictions (*this will happen*) where she would normally hedge. Stops asking questions in meetings; asks only confirmatory ones. Begins quoting her own prior statements as precedent.
*Interpersonal:* Splitting is now operational. Former peers are sorted into *with* or *obstructing*. The sorting is sticky — once a peer is reclassified as obstruction, returning them to peer status requires a discrete repair event, not the passage of time. Disagreement is processed as *information about the disagreer*, not about the question. Mentees are protected ferociously and *kept out of the room* where the hard calls are being made; she will not let Kamala see the worst of it, which is itself diagnostic — she knows what she is becoming and is curating witnesses.
*Operational:* Preemption. Acts on predicted rather than realized threat. Detentions, perimeter expansions, override of normal procedure under "extraordinary circumstances" framing. Will not be the one to call a stand-down meeting; if one is called, she arrives late and leaves early.

**Rung 5 — Decompensation Proper.**
Historically rare and historically *retroactive*. The Warbird-era alcoholic collapse is the cleanest example; the post-CWII isolation is the more recent. The pattern is **a single discrete catastrophic act or revealed condition** that resolves the pressure by removing her from the field — either because she has done something undefendable, because her body has stopped permitting it, or because the people who would otherwise normalize her behavior have finally withdrawn.
*Warbird template:* impaired flight during *Live Kree or Dead*, near-loss of civilians, court-martial, exit from team, bottom, rebuild. The *bottom* was not visible to her until she was sitting in it.
*CWII template:* the dead partner, the comatose colleague, the fractured community, the final fight with Stark — *and only then* the long, quiet isolation in which the accountability work could begin.
*Brain-lesion template:* she flew the mission knowing the cost. The "decompensation" was the willing self-erasure of recent memory. Read in this file as a *sublimated* version of the same pattern — she paid the cost to her own continuity rather than to a relationship or a civilian, but it is structurally the same act: a discrete catastrophic resolution she chose over a slow honest negotiation with limit.

---

### 6.2 The Specific Conditions That Produce Escalation

Not all stress moves her up the ladder. The triggers are specific and almost entirely traceable to the trauma signature mapped in §3.

**Trigger Class A — Bodily/Autonomy Violations to Self or Proxies.**
Highest-amplitude trigger. Any scenario that rhymes with the Marcus event — coerced reproduction, body-puppeting, mind-control, possession, identity-theft, non-consensual modification — moves her two rungs in one step. The proxy effect matters: a young woman being subjected to such a thing in her vicinity will trigger the same response as if it were happening to her, and she will not differentiate the response intensity. Mission-planning should anticipate that any operation involving such a threat-class will be conducted by a Danvers operating at minimum Rung 3 from briefing onward.

**Trigger Class B — Failure of Witness by Chosen Family.**
The Avengers-applauding-her-captor template. *Specifically:* peers failing to see harm being done to her or to someone she has positioned as protected. Not disagreement — disagreement is tolerated at lower rungs. *Failure to see.* If she perceives that Jessica, Rhodey (historically), Monica, or Kamala has missed something she considers obvious and harmful, the response is disproportionate distancing followed by — characteristically — a long delay before any repair attempt. Tony is a special case here: the Stark relationship has been *both* the intervention that saved her life (Warbird) and the failure of witness that broke her trust (CWII). The relationship oscillates because both templates are live.

**Trigger Class C — Diminishment of Capability.**
Power loss, injury, benching, or the *implication* that she should accept reduced operational latitude. Activates the Warbird substrate — the era of being a lesser version of herself among people who had seen her cosmic. She knows this trigger now (post-Stohl integration) and watches for it. The watching produces a characteristic behavior: she will *volunteer* to step back from a mission in low-stakes contexts to prove to herself she can, and then refuse to step back from a high-stakes one *because* she has been proving she can. The pattern is self-aware but not self-corrected.

**Trigger Class D — Father-Coded Authority Demanding Stand-Down.**
Male authority figures, particularly older and structurally senior, telling her to halt or defer. Joseph Danvers is the template. The reflex is *not to comply*, and the reflex is faster than the assessment. This trigger is interesting because she has spent forty years inside hierarchical institutions (USAF, NASA, Avengers, the SHIELD-adjacent apparatus, Alpha Flight Space Program) precisely so she can be the authority — but when she encounters it in another, the original wiring fires. The CWII confrontations with Stark were dense with this dynamic, regardless of whether Stark himself was wielding authority or grief.

**Trigger Class E — Mentees in Preventable Danger.**
The Kamala wire. A young person, particularly a young woman, in harm she could have foreseen and forestalled. Produces the highest-velocity ascent on the ladder of any trigger class — she can move from Rung 2 to Rung 4 within a single scene. This is the trigger that originally generated the CWII detention logic and remains the most likely route to future overreach. Notably, *Kamala herself* arguing against the overreach was not sufficient to interrupt the pattern — the trigger and the corrective came from the same person, and the trigger won.

**Trigger Class F — Maternal/Origin Disclosures.**
Activated late in the published record (*Life of CM*). Any revelation that reframes who she is at the constitutional level — Kree heritage, hidden parentage, retconned biology — moves her through a different and slower escalation pattern: not toward operational hardening but toward withdrawal, retreat to the family home, manual labor (the house renovations in Stohl's run are not incidental), and a period of refusing the uniform. This is the *only* trigger class that consistently produces a *deceleration* rather than acceleration response, and it is therapeutic in net effect. Worth noting for handlers: putting her in contact with the Harpswell Sound house, with her brothers, with the matrilineal artifacts, is the closest thing in the file to a reliable downregulator.

---

### 6.3 The Sobriety Variable — Load-Bearing and Brittle

The sobriety, intact since the late-1990s arc, is the single most important behavioral fact in this entire dossier and must be understood as a *structural* feature, not merely a health outcome.

It is load-bearing in three ways. First, it is the discipline that contains the affect-regulation deficit identified in §3 — she cannot drink, so the energy that would have gone to drinking goes to *work, control, perimeter-management*. Second, it is the proof-of-self she carries into every confrontation about her judgment: she has been wrong, she has hit a bottom, she has rebuilt, she has stayed sober through events that broke other Avengers (Rhodey's death, the CWII fallout, the brain lesion). Third, it is the moral floor of her self-concept — *I am someone who does the hard thing and does not flinch* — and that floor cannot crack without the whole structure shifting.

The brittleness follows directly. Because sobriety is doing this much work, *any* threat to it is processed at maximum priority. She does not appear to be tempted in the conventional sense — there is no published evidence of craving, no near-relapse scenes, no white-knuckling at functions where alcohol is served. The discipline is so total it has become invisible. But the *price* of that totality is that the same all-or-nothing cognitive style which protects the sobriety also generates the operational rigidities described above. You cannot have one without the other; the personality structure that holds the sobriety is the personality structure that produces the CWII.

Two specific behavioral consequences:
- *She will not drink even when drinking would be the smaller mistake.* In contexts where a peer might decompress with a glass of wine and avoid a larger eruption, she will go directly to the larger eruption.
- *She is unusually intolerant of others' substance use under operational stress.* Read this not as moralism but as projection of her own load-bearing wall — if drinking is what undisciplined people do, and she cannot be undisciplined, she cannot be near it without the framing destabilizing.

The single most concerning scenario the file can imagine for this subject is one in which sobriety itself is somehow compromised against her will — a coerced intoxication, a possession that uses her body to drink, a body-double scenario in which she is publicly seen drinking. The Marcus template overlays the sobriety template; the response would be at the upper bound of what she is capable of.

---

### 6.4 What Collapse Actually Looks Like

Not the dramatic version. The actual version, drawn from canon:

**The Warbird shape.** Not staggering and slurring on missions — though that did happen — but *the inability to recognize that the staggering and slurring is the thing other people are seeing*. She flew the mission. She believed she was flying it well. The gap between her self-assessment and her performance was the collapse; the impaired flight was merely the surface. When Stark named the gap, the response was rage, then exit, then a long invisibility, then return. There was no soft middle. There never is.

**The CWII shape.** Not screaming and breaking things — she rarely does this — but *the steady, articulate, militarily-coherent defense of a position that is destroying her relationships and her standing while she continues to defend it*. The decompensation was not affective. It was the *failure of the reality-testing loop with peers* that should have flagged the position as untenable. Peers raised the flag. She reclassified them. The collapse was the reclassification, not anything that happened afterward.

**The brain-lesion shape.** Not failure to act — *the choice to act at the cost of self*. She flew the mission knowing she would lose the memory. Read in this file as a *controlled* decompensation: she found a way to pay the price in personal continuity rather than in others' safety or in her sobriety. This is the *best version* of her collapse pattern and shows what the integrated form looks like — she will still spend herself to zero, but she has learned to direct the spending.

**The post-CWII shape.** Withdrawal. Not depression in the clinical sense — she is not anhedonic, not vegetative — but a long, deliberate stepping-back from the rooms in which she had previously been central. The accountability work is real and largely private. The repair with Stark, with Jessica, with Kamala happens slowly, one person at a time, and requires *her* to initiate, which she does, late and awkwardly but correctly. The collapse was the CWII itself; what followed was metabolism.

Across all four shapes, the common feature: **she does not signal distress before the catastrophic act, and she does signal it after.** Handlers who wait for her to ask for help will wait until after the damage. Handlers who try to read the ladder in real time and intervene at Rung 3 have a chance.

---

### 6.5 What Does Not Break Her

A negative inventory, equally important.

- *Physical pain.* She has been tortured, irradiated, depowered, body-stolen, and impaled. None of it produces decompensation; some of it produces operational improvement. Pain is data.
- *Numerical disadvantage.* Being outgunned, outnumbered, or out-leveraged tends to *lower* her rung, not raise it — she becomes more present, more humorous, more recognizably herself in fights she should lose. The Binary-era deep-space arcs show this consistently.
- *Public criticism.* She is indifferent to opinion outside her chosen-family circle. Press, political pressure, hero-community grumbling — noise. She does not read it. The CWII catastrophe was not driven by public response; she would have done the same thing in private.
- *Being wrong, eventually.* Once the conviction-under-pressure has resolved (usually via a discrete catastrophic act), she can absorb being wrong. The post-CWII accountability is real. The Stohl-run integration of her Kree heritage required her to revise her self-concept at the constitutional level and she did it. *Slow* corrigibility is genuine. *Fast* corrigibility under live pressure is the problem.

---

### 6.6 Conditions Required for Worst-Case Decompensation

Synthesizing the above, the file identifies the conditions under which Danvers is most likely to produce a Category-1 incident — defined here as an action of such operational scale and moral weight that it fractures the wider hero community and produces casualties or detentions that cannot be undone.

The conditions are:
1. A mentee or proxy-daughter figure in foreseeable danger (Trigger E live).
2. A peer or peer-group already classed as obstruction (Trigger B latent, splitting active).
3. A predictive or precognitive information source she finds credible (the CWII precondition — *she will act on forecast*).
4. A father-coded authority figure available to push against (Trigger D live; sharpens the refusal-reflex).
5. A high-tempo operational rhythm preventing sleep, meals, and contact with the matrilineal/Harpswell downregulator (Trigger F suppressed).
6. Sobriety intact and load-bearing — *which it will be*; this is constant.

When five or more of these conditions are met simultaneously, the file's prediction is that Danvers will escalate to Rung 4 within seventy-two hours and to a discrete catastrophic act within two weeks. Intervention must occur at the condition-level (remove one of the six) rather than at the behavior-level (argue with her at Rung 4 — historically ineffective and frequently counterproductive).

---

### 6.7 The Charitable and Necessary Last Word

She is, by the standards of this cohort, *one of the more functional* trauma survivors on file. She has integrated more than most. She is sober, she mentors well, she can be wrong and recover, she has done the matrilineal work, she has chosen self-erasure over civilian harm. The pattern documented here is not pathology in any conventional sense — it is the cost-structure of a competent, traumatized, sober commander who has built a self out of refusal and who will spend that self, repeatedly, in service of not being the small girl her father told she could not.

The dossier's failure-mode analysis exists not to indict but to make her *workable* — to give the people who care about her, and the institutions she serves, the granularity needed to intervene early, to read the ladder honestly, and to absorb the withdrawal long enough to bring her back. She has demonstrated, across every documented collapse, the capacity to come back. The work is in shortening the distance between the catastrophic act and the metabolism that follows it — and, where possible, in catching her at Rung 3, before the discrete act becomes necessary to her at all.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# SECTION 12 — TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

*UATU file CMD-616, longitudinal projection module. Confidence levels noted parenthetically. All forecasts are conditional on continued operational tempo at or above current baseline; subject does not metabolize peacetime well, which is itself a finding.*

---

## 12.1 The Shape of the Curve

Read across her full published life, the subject's trajectory is not linear but *spiral*: she returns to the same coordinates — diminishment, overreach, isolation, rebuild — at successively higher altitudes of capability and self-knowledge. The error rate does not drop to zero; the *recognition latency* drops. Where in the Warbird era she required external intervention and total collapse to register that something was wrong, by post-*Civil War II* she was naming her own overreach in months rather than years, and by the post-Stohl integration she is capable, at her best, of catching the pattern mid-deployment. This is the single most important fact about her forward arc. **She is getting faster at finding herself, not better at not losing herself.** (HIGH CONFIDENCE.)

The implication for the next decade of operational life is that her catastrophes will be *shorter and sharper* rather than longer and softer. Expect acute crises — a forty-eight-hour bad decision, a single mission that fractures a relationship — rather than the multi-year Warbird-style descent. The shape changes; the substrate does not.

---

## 12.2 The Three Forks

Forward assessment resolves into three high-leverage decision-points the subject will almost certainly face. Each has a growth-vector and a catastrophe-vector; the difference between them is rarely the situation and almost always the company she is keeping when it arrives.

### Fork 1: The Next Preemption Event (Likelihood: NEAR-CERTAIN within 24 months of operational tempo)

The Civil War II logic — *I have foreknowledge, therefore I have obligation, therefore dissent is obstruction* — is not a one-time error. It is the predictable output of her operational code (act first; authority over ambiguity; mentees-in-danger as override condition) meeting any future information asymmetry that hands her seeming-certainty. The asymmetry need not be precognitive; it can be intelligence product, Kree-derived foresight, a Reed Richards probability engine, an Eternals-scale forecast, or simply a tactical read she trusts more than the consensus around her. The wire is the same.

- **Growth vector.** She enters the situation with at least one peer pre-authorized to call the stop — a standing agreement, made in calm, that some specific named person can order her to pause and she has pre-committed to comply. Kamala is structurally wrong for this role (the mentee cannot be the brake without breaking the relationship; the CWII shape revealed exactly this). Jessica Drew is structurally correct; Monica Rambeau is structurally correct; Rhodey, when present, was structurally correct and his absence is part of why CWII metastasized. If she has built this scaffolding before the fork, she clears it. (MODERATE confidence she will.)
- **Catastrophe vector.** She enters alone, command-burdened, recently grieving, and operating on information no one else can verify. Under those conditions she will repeat the error with a near-100% probability, and the second occurrence will cost her the community standing that absorbed the first. There is no third CWII; the cohort will not extend that grace twice.

### Fork 2: The Power Question (Likelihood: HIGH within the decade)

Her relationship to her own power is the unresolved center of her arc. The Binary-Warbird oscillation is the canonical version; the brain lesion and chosen amnesia is the DeConnick-era version; the Kree-heritage revelation is the Stohl-era version. The next iteration is structurally overdue and will likely take one of three forms: (a) a power *escalation* that returns her to or past Binary levels and forces the question of whether she remains an Avenger or becomes a cosmic-scale agent in her own right; (b) a power *loss or constraint* that returns her to the Warbird substrate under sober conditions for the first time; (c) a power *transformation* via further Kree integration that asks her to choose how human she wishes to remain.

- **Growth vector across all three.** She metabolizes the change through the mentorship and matrilineal frames she has built — Kamala on one side, the integrated memory of Marie on the other. The power becomes a thing she *has* rather than a thing she *is*, which is the work *Life of Captain Marvel* began and did not finish.
- **Catastrophe vector.** Escalation without containment recapitulates the Binary self-exile (she leaves Earth, ostensibly for scale-appropriate threats, actually because intimacy at human scale has become unbearable against the new altitude). Loss without containment is the most dangerous scenario in this entire file: a sober Carol Danvers at Warbird capability, with twenty more years of command identity, no permitted self-medication, and no Tony Stark in the recovery chair, is a person whose rigidity has nowhere to go. The probability of an unhealthy compensatory behavior — not drinking; something else, likely overwork to physiological injury, or a return to military structure at the cost of independent judgment — is high. Watch for: enlistment-coded language, uniform-coded dress drift, increased deference to chain-of-command framings she would previously have questioned.

### Fork 3: The Succession Question (Likelihood: CERTAIN, timing variable)

She has been preparing Kamala Khan to inherit the mantle since 2014, whether or not she has fully admitted it to herself. The succession is the test she has been training for: can she hand the name *Captain Marvel* to someone else while she is still alive, still capable, and still wanted in the role? This is the inverse of every prior identity transition in her file. Ms. Marvel → Binary was forced by trauma. Binary → Warbird was forced by power decay. Warbird → Captain Marvel was earned through grief over Mar-Vell and the *House of M* counterfactual. Captain Marvel → ? is the first one she would have to *choose*.

- **Growth vector.** She survives the handoff and discovers a self underneath the mantle. This is the *integration* end-state the entire arc has been climbing toward: Carol Danvers as a person who once was Captain Marvel, who is now something else — possibly a teacher, possibly a cosmic-affairs ambassador, possibly a writer of the memoir she has refused to write — and who finds that the small girl in Boston was not so unbearable to be after all. This is the Malcolm-at-Mecca structural beat: the late-life reframe that contextualizes everything prior. (LOW-TO-MODERATE confidence she gets here, but it is the available end-state.)
- **Catastrophe vector.** She cannot let go. She either refuses the succession outright (and damages Kamala in the refusal), or she performs the succession publicly while continuing to occupy the role functionally (the worst version: a mentor who will not vacate the cockpit). Watch for: increased proprietary language about the callsign; resistance to Kamala operating without consultation; reframings of mentee independence as recklessness requiring correction.

---

## 12.3 The Open Questions

Five things the file cannot currently resolve and which will determine which fork she takes.

1. **Does she ever sit with the Marcus event in a clinical setting?** Across decades of canon she has named it, raged about it, and moved on; there is no evidence of sustained therapeutic work on the core wound. She has *integrated* it functionally — through Claremont's corrective, through mentorship, through the matrilineal arc — but integration is not metabolization. The wire is still live. The open question is whether she ever encounters a context safe enough and slow enough to do the work that mission-immersion has substituted for. If she does, the CWII vector loses most of its charge. If she does not, the vector remains armed for life.

2. **What happens to her sobriety under a stress event that exceeds prior worst-case?** She has held the line through Rhodey's death, through the brain lesion, through the loss of recent memory, through community ostracism after CWII. The line has held because the line is load-bearing — sobriety is identity, not behavior. The open question is whether there is a stress event large enough to crack the wall, and what comes out if it does. Probability of relapse in any given year is genuinely low (HIGH confidence); probability across thirty more operational years under escalating stakes is non-trivial. The relapse, if it comes, will not look like the Warbird arc. It will be quieter, faster, and likelier to be caught — *if* her chosen family is still close enough to see it.

3. **Is the chosen family still close enough to see it?** Post-CWII attrition is real. Jessica Drew is the keystone relationship; the Drew relationship's depth across decades is the single best prognostic indicator in the file. If that relationship survives the next preemption event intact, the entire prognosis improves. If it does not — if Jessica is the one she loses next, by death or by withdrawal — the system loses its most reliable corrective and the catastrophe vectors all gain probability.

4. **Does she ever build a life outside the mission?** The DeConnick run gestured at it (the apartment above the bar, the cat, the chosen-family rituals); the subsequent runs collapsed it back into operational tempo. The open question is whether she is capable of *sustained* off-duty existence or whether peacetime is, for her, a kind of slow injury. The Banshee-bar period is the most important data point here, and the fact that it did not durably stick is concerning. Watch for: whether she ever takes leave that is not medically or politically forced.

5. **What does she do with the Kree question long-term?** The Stohl-era revelation is recent in arc-time and unresolved in identity-time. She has not yet had to make a *political* choice about Kree affiliation under conditions of conflict. When she does — and a Kree-Earth crisis is a near-certain feature of any decade of operational tempo — the question of which side of her heritage commands her loyalty will be forced. The healthy answer is *both, conditionally, with the conditions named*. The unhealthy answer is the splitting-under-stress pattern weaponized at species scale.

---

## 12.4 Leading Indicators — What To Watch

Granular behavioral tells that, in the historical record, have preceded each major decompensation. These are the early-warning panel.

- **Language drift toward the declarative.** When her speech pattern compresses — shorter sentences, more imperatives, fewer hedges, increased use of *we will* and *I need you to* — she is climbing the stress ladder. This is the most reliable single indicator. Three-week trend is meaningful; three-month trend is actionable.
- **Reduction in casual physical contact.** Baseline Carol is a back-slapper, a shoulder-grabber, a hug-initiator with the small circle. Pre-decompensation Carol is hands-to-self, arms-crossed at briefings, body angled toward exits. The Warbird-era visual record is unambiguous on this.
- **Sleep-cycle compression.** Her training tolerates short sleep; her psychology does not. When operational tempo drives her under five hours sustained, judgment narrows toward preemption within ten to fourteen days. Historically uncorrelated with caffeine intake (she will not increase it; she treats stimulants as an unearned shortcut), correlated with increased solo flight time at altitude. The flying-alone-at-night pattern is a self-soothing behavior and a warning sign simultaneously.
- **Withdrawal from Jessica Drew specifically.** Not from the group; from Jessica. When she stops returning Jessica's calls, the system is in trouble. Jessica is the canary; the cohort should be briefed accordingly.
- **Increased reference to her father in unprompted contexts.** The Joseph Danvers material surfaces in her speech almost exclusively when the original wound is being touched by current events. Spontaneous mention is diagnostic.
- **Uniform-coded dress drift off-duty.** When she begins wearing the flight jacket to civilian functions she would previously have dressed down for, the role is consuming the person. This is subtle and easy to miss; it is also one of the most reliable indicators that the integration work is slipping.
- **Refusal of medical follow-up.** She tolerates medical attention immediately post-mission; she resists scheduled follow-up. The resistance scales with how much she fears the result. A pattern of cancelled neurological appointments would be a five-alarm signal given the lesion history.
- **Mentorship overreach toward Kamala.** When she begins second-guessing Kamala's operational choices in real-time over comms rather than debriefing afterward, the succession vector is going wrong. This is the specific behavior to flag.

---

## 12.5 The Conditions of Growth

What would actually move her forward, stated as concretely as the file permits.

1. **A peer authorized to stop her, named in advance, and used at least once successfully.** The single highest-leverage intervention available. The success of the first use is more important than its content; she needs the lived experience of being stopped by chosen family and surviving it without rupture. Without this, every preemption fork resolves the wrong way.

2. **Sustained off-duty existence, defended against her own attempts to dissolve it.** Six months. A cat. A neighbor whose name she knows. A standing dinner she does not cancel. The Banshee-bar period proved she is capable of this; the subsequent collapse proved she will not maintain it without external structure. The structure should be social, not medical.

3. **Therapeutic work on the Marcus event, conducted slowly, with a practitioner who is not also a colleague.** The closest historical analog in the cohort is Tony's recovery work, which she observed and rejected as a model for herself because accepting it would mean accepting the diagnosis. The pathway in is not framing it as treatment; it is framing it as training. She will sit for *training* she will not sit for *therapy*. Whoever brings her the door should know which sign to put on it.

4. **A successful, completed handoff of the Captain Marvel mantle to Kamala, performed when Carol is still capable of holding it.** Voluntary succession from strength is the integration-end-state. Involuntary succession from injury or death is the catastrophe-end-state. The window for the former is finite and closes earlier than she will want it to.

5. **A reconciliation with Tony Stark that names the CWII rupture, the intervention rupture, and the Marcus-era failure-of-witness in a single conversation.** None of the three are individually adequate to repair the relationship; together they are. This is unlikely to occur without an external precipitating event; when it does occur, it will be the most consequential single conversation of her late-career life.

---

## 12.6 The Conditions of Catastrophe

The mirror image. What would route her to the worst available outcome.

1. **The death of Jessica Drew.** Removes the keystone corrective. Probability of subsequent decompensation within twenty-four months is high; shape is most likely a Binary-style self-exile reframed as a cosmic-affairs posting, with Earth-side relationships maintained at correspondence-distance only.

2. **A second preemption event treated by the community as a second strike.** Loss of cohort standing she has spent post-CWII years rebuilding. Drives her toward subordinate structures that will accept her unconditionally — Alpha Flight, S.W.O.R.D., a Kree affiliation. The structural problem with all three is that they reward her authoritarian substrate rather than constraining it.

3. **An injury to Kamala Khan that Carol believes she could have prevented.** This is the single highest-magnitude wire in her current emotional architecture. The Rhodey-CWII pattern would recur at higher intensity and with less available correction, because Kamala occupies the daughter-coded slot that Rhodey did not. The aftermath would not be a policy overreach; it would be personal, sustained, and aimed at whoever Carol identified as proximate cause.

4. **Forced return to a non-sober environment under operational requirement.** A long-term undercover assignment, a diplomatic posting requiring social drinking, a captivity scenario in which alcohol is the available coping resource. Her sobriety is not white-knuckled but it is also not battle-tested against environmental immersion. This is the most underappreciated risk in the file.

5. **A Kree-Earth war in which she is asked to choose sides publicly.** Splits the integrated identity along the seam Stohl welded. Either choice damages her; the damage of refusing to choose is greater than the damage of either side.

---

## 12.7 Terminal Assessment

The subject's life, read forward, is a question about whether a person constructed almost entirely out of refusal can learn to build out of acceptance instead — not the acceptance of her wounds, which she has, but the acceptance of *being held* by people who can see her without requiring her to be the one seeing first. Every growth vector in this file routes through that capacity. Every catastrophe vector routes around it.

She will not collapse. The structural rigidity that makes catastrophe possible also makes total collapse unlikely; she is too disciplined, too sober, too well-defended, and too genuinely good at the job. She will, instead, keep narrowing — unless something or someone widens her. The widening will not come from a mission. It will come, if it comes, from a Tuesday afternoon she did not schedule, a conversation she did not control, a moment in which the small girl from Boston is permitted in the room with the woman who has spent fifty years refusing to be her.

The probability that she finds that afternoon is, on the current evidence, roughly even. The probability that she is worth the cohort's patience while she looks for it is, on the same evidence, considerably higher than that.

*— UATU, file closes pending next operational data.*

## Relationship Graph
### [[Jessica Campbell Jones (Jewel (retired); Knightress (briefly); Power Woman (briefly))]]
- Her best friend and the other drinker — the one person who sees straight through the armor and refuses to be impressed by the rank. Jess is the relationship where Carol is closest to unarmored, which is exactly why it matters and why she protects it.

### [[Tony Stark (Iron Man)]]
- Civil War II: Carol, acting on precrime certainty, beat Tony into a coma — the friendship she incinerated rather than tolerate the doubt that she might be wrong. The defining proof that her righteousness costs the people closest to her.

### [[Anna Marie LeBeau (Rogue)]]
- Rogue once absorbed Carol's powers, memories, and self wholesale, leaving her an emptied shell. For a woman whose core was already thin, having it literally stolen is the deepest violation; the entanglement between them is canon and unhealed.

### [[Mar-Vell (Captain Marvel / Protector of the Universe / Walter Lawson)]]
- The original Captain Marvel whose name and legacy she carries. The mantle is both honor and burden — another external structure she wears to hold a self that has no internal frame.
